## 7. FILE SYSTEM IMPLEMENTATION DETAILS

### 7.1 File System Parser Architecture

```rust
/// Core file system abstraction
pub trait FileSystemParser: Send + Sync {
    /// Get file system type
    fn fs_type(&self) -> FileSystemType;
    
    /// Parse file system and load metadata
    fn parse(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<FSMetadata>;
    
    /// Get file allocation map (which sectors are used)
    fn get_allocation_map(&self) -> AllocationMap;
    
    /// Look up file metadata by inode/reference
    fn lookup_file(&self, inode: u64) 
        -> Result<Option<FileMetadata>>;
    
    /// Get deleted file entries (if available)
    fn get_deleted_entries(&self) -> Vec<DeletedFileEntry>;
    
    /// Get journal/log entries (if available)
    fn get_journal_entries(&self) 
        -> Vec<JournalEntry>;
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum FileSystemType {
    NTFS,
    HFSPlus,
    APFS,
    EXT2,
    EXT3,
    EXT4,
    FAT12,
    FAT16,
    FAT32,
    ExFAT,
    Btrfs,
    XFS,
}

pub struct FSMetadata {
    pub fs_type: FileSystemType,
    pub total_size: u64,
    pub used_size: u64,
    pub free_size: u64,
    pub block_size: u32,
    pub creation_time: u64,
    pub modification_time: u64,
}

pub struct AllocationMap {
    /// Bitmap or vector indicating allocated vs free sectors
    pub allocations: Vec<bool>,
    pub sector_size: usize,
}

pub struct DeletedFileEntry {
    pub original_name: String,
    pub original_size: u64,
    pub deletion_time: Option<u64>,
    pub first_cluster: u64,
    pub metadata: FileMetadata,
}

pub struct JournalEntry {
    pub timestamp: u64,
    pub operation: JournalOperation,
    pub affected_inode: Option<u64>,
    pub details: String,
}

pub enum JournalOperation {
    FileCreated,
    FileDeleted,
    FileModified,
    MetadataChanged,
    TransactionCommit,
}

pub struct FileMetadata {
    pub inode: u64,
    pub name: String,
    pub size: u64,
    pub created: u64,
    pub modified: u64,
    pub accessed: u64,
    pub permissions: u32,
    pub owner_uid: Option<u32>,
    pub owner_gid: Option<u32>,
    pub is_directory: bool,
    pub is_symlink: bool,
    pub allocation_blocks: Vec<BlockRange>,
}

pub struct BlockRange {
    pub start_block: u64,
    pub num_blocks: u64,
}
```

### 7.1.1 NTFS Parser Implementation

```rust
use std::mem;

pub struct NTFSParser {
    boot_sector: [u8; 512],
    mft_entries: Vec<MFTEntry>,
    cluster_size: u32,
    sectors_per_cluster: u32,
    bytes_per_sector: u16,
}

#[repr(C)]
pub struct NTFSBootSector {
    pub jump: [u8; 3],
    pub oem_id: [u8; 8],
    pub bytes_per_sector: u16,
    pub sectors_per_cluster: u8,
    pub reserved_sectors: u16,
    pub fats: u8,
    pub root_entries: u16,
    pub total_sectors: u16,
    pub media_descriptor: u8,
    pub sectors_per_fat: u16,
    pub sectors_per_track: u16,
    pub num_heads: u16,
    pub hidden_sectors: u32,
    pub total_sectors_large: u32,
    pub reserved: [u8; 48],
    pub total_sectors_ntfs: u64,
    pub mft_logical_cluster: u64,
    pub mft_mirror_lcn: u64,
    pub clusters_per_mft_record: u8,
    pub clusters_per_index_record: u8,
    pub serial_number: u64,
}

pub struct MFTEntry {
    pub record_number: u64,
    pub size: u32,
    pub data: Vec<u8>,
    pub is_directory: bool,
    pub filename: String,
    pub file_size: u64,
    pub allocated_size: u64,
    pub creation_time: u64,
    pub modification_time: u64,
    pub accessed_time: u64,
    pub flags: u32,
}

impl NTFSParser {
    pub fn new(device: &dyn StorageDevice) -> Result<Self> {
        // Read boot sector
        let boot_data = device.read_sectors(0, 1)?;
        let mut boot_sector = [0u8; 512];
        boot_sector.copy_from_slice(&boot_data[..512]);
        
        let ptr = &boot_sector as *const u8 
            as *const NTFSBootSector;
        let boot = unsafe { ptr.as_ref().unwrap() };
        
        // Validate NTFS signature
        if &boot_sector[3..11] != b"NTFS    " {
            return Err("Invalid NTFS boot sector".into());
        }
        
        let cluster_size = (boot.sectors_per_cluster as u32) 
            * (boot.bytes_per_sector as u32);
        
        Ok(NTFSParser {
            boot_sector,
            mft_entries: Vec::new(),
            cluster_size,
            sectors_per_cluster: boot.sectors_per_cluster as u32,
            bytes_per_sector: boot.bytes_per_sector,
        })
    }
    
    pub fn parse_mft(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<()> {
        let boot_ptr = &self.boot_sector as *const u8 
            as *const NTFSBootSector;
        let boot = unsafe { boot_ptr.as_ref().unwrap() };
        
        // MFT location in logical clusters
        let mft_lcn = boot.mft_logical_cluster;
        let mft_byte_offset = mft_lcn * self.cluster_size as u64;
        
        // Read MFT records
        let mft_record_size = 
            (boot.clusters_per_mft_record as u32) * self.cluster_size;
        
        // Read first 100 MFT records (configurable)
        let num_records_to_read = 100;
        
        for i in 0..num_records_to_read {
            let offset = mft_byte_offset 
                + (i as u64 * mft_record_size as u64);
            
            match device.read_bytes(offset, mft_record_size as usize) {
                Ok(data) => {
                    if let Ok(entry) = self.parse_mft_record(&data, i) {
                        self.mft_entries.push(entry);
                    }
                }
                Err(_) => break, // End of readable MFT
            }
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn parse_mft_record(&self, data: &[u8], record_num: u32) 
        -> Result<MFTEntry> {
        if data.len() < 42 {
            return Err("MFT record too small".into());
        }
        
        // Check signature "FILE"
        if &data[0..4] != b"FILE" {
            return Err("Invalid MFT record signature".into());
        }
        
        // Parse attributes
        let filename = self.extract_filename_attribute(data)
            .unwrap_or_default();
        let file_size = self.extract_data_attribute_size(data)
            .unwrap_or(0);
        let is_directory = (data[22] & 0x02) != 0;
        
        Ok(MFTEntry {
            record_number: record_num as u64,
            size: data.len() as u32,
            data: data.to_vec(),
            is_directory,
            filename,
            file_size,
            allocated_size: 0, // Calculate from attributes
            creation_time: 0,
            modification_time: 0,
            accessed_time: 0,
            flags: u32::from_le_bytes([data[22], data[23], 0, 0]),
        })
    }
    
    fn extract_filename_attribute(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Option<String> {
        // Find filename attribute (type 0x40)
        let mut offset = 20;
        
        while offset < data.len() {
            if offset + 4 > data.len() {
                break;
            }
            
            let attr_type = u32::from_le_bytes([
                data[offset], data[offset + 1], 
                data[offset + 2], data[offset + 3]
            ]);
            
            if attr_type == 0xFFFFFFFF {
                break; // End marker
            }
            
            if attr_type == 0x40 {
                // Filename attribute found
                // Parse filename from attribute
                if let Some(name) = self.parse_filename_attr(&data[offset..]) {
                    return Some(name);
                }
            }
            
            // Move to next attribute
            let attr_len = u32::from_le_bytes([
                data[offset + 4], data[offset + 5],
                data[offset + 6], data[offset + 7]
            ]) as usize;
            
            offset += attr_len;
        }
        
        None
    }
    
    fn extract_data_attribute_size(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Option<u64> {
        let mut offset = 20;
        
        while offset < data.len() {
            if offset + 4 > data.len() {
                break;
            }
            
            let attr_type = u32::from_le_bytes([
                data[offset], data[offset + 1],
                data[offset + 2], data[offset + 3]
            ]);
            
            if attr_type == 0xFFFFFFFF {
                break;
            }
            
            if attr_type == 0x80 {
                // Data attribute
                // Size is at offset 48-56 within attribute
                if offset + 56 < data.len() {
                    return Some(u64::from_le_bytes(
                        data[offset + 48..offset + 56]
                            .try_into()
                            .unwrap_or([0; 8])
                    ));
                }
            }
            
            let attr_len = u32::from_le_bytes([
                data[offset + 4], data[offset + 5],
                data[offset + 6], data[offset + 7]
            ]) as usize;
            
            offset += attr_len;
        }
        
        None
    }
    
    fn parse_filename_attr(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Option<String> {
        // Filename is stored as UTF-16 in the attribute
        if data.len() < 66 {
            return None;
        }
        
        let name_len = data[64] as usize;
        if name_len == 0 || data.len() < 66 + name_len * 2 {
            return None;
        }
        
        let name_bytes = &data[66..66 + name_len * 2];
        
        // Decode UTF-16 LE
        let mut name = String::new();
        for i in (0..name_bytes.len()).step_by(2) {
            let code_unit = u16::from_le_bytes([
                name_bytes[i],
                if i + 1 < name_bytes.len() { name_bytes[i + 1] } else { 0 }
            ]);
            
            if code_unit == 0 {
                break;
            }
            
            if let Some(c) = char::from_u32(code_unit as u32) {
                name.push(c);
            }
        }
        
        if name.is_empty() {
            None
        } else {
            Some(name)
        }
    }
}

impl FileSystemParser for NTFSParser {
    fn fs_type(&self) -> FileSystemType {
        FileSystemType::NTFS
    }
    
    fn parse(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<FSMetadata> {
        self.parse_mft(device)?;
        
        let boot_ptr = &self.boot_sector as *const u8 
            as *const NTFSBootSector;
        let boot = unsafe { boot_ptr.as_ref().unwrap() };
        
        Ok(FSMetadata {
            fs_type: FileSystemType::NTFS,
            total_size: boot.total_sectors_ntfs * self.bytes_per_sector as u64,
            used_size: 0, // Calculate from allocation map
            free_size: 0,
            block_size: self.cluster_size,
            creation_time: 0,
            modification_time: 0,
        })
    }
    
    fn get_allocation_map(&self) -> AllocationMap {
        AllocationMap {
            allocations: Vec::new(), // Implement bitmap reading
            sector_size: self.bytes_per_sector as usize,
        }
    }
    
    fn lookup_file(&self, inode: u64) 
        -> Result<Option<FileMetadata>> {
        if let Some(mft_entry) = 
            self.mft_entries.iter().find(|e| e.record_number == inode) {
            Ok(Some(FileMetadata {
                inode,
                name: mft_entry.filename.clone(),
                size: mft_entry.file_size,
                created: mft_entry.creation_time,
                modified: mft_entry.modification_time,
                accessed: mft_entry.accessed_time,
                permissions: 0o644,
                owner_uid: None,
                owner_gid: None,
                is_directory: mft_entry.is_directory,
                is_symlink: false,
                allocation_blocks: Vec::new(),
            }))
        } else {
            Ok(None)
        }
    }
    
    fn get_deleted_entries(&self) -> Vec<DeletedFileEntry> {
        self.mft_entries
            .iter()
            .filter(|entry| (entry.flags & 0x01) == 0) // Not in use
            .map(|entry| DeletedFileEntry {
                original_name: entry.filename.clone(),
                original_size: entry.file_size,
                deletion_time: None,
                first_cluster: 0,
                metadata: FileMetadata {
                    inode: entry.record_number,
                    name: entry.filename.clone(),
                    size: entry.file_size,
                    created: entry.creation_time,
                    modified: entry.modification_time,
                    accessed: entry.accessed_time,
                    permissions: 0o644,
                    owner_uid: None,
                    owner_gid: None,
                    is_directory: entry.is_directory,
                    is_symlink: false,
                    allocation_blocks: Vec::new(),
                },
            })
            .collect()
    }
    
    fn get_journal_entries(&self) -> Vec<JournalEntry> {
        Vec::new() // Implement journal parsing
    }
}
```

### 7.1.2 EXT4 Parser Implementation

```rust
pub struct EXT4Parser {
    superblock: EXT4Superblock,
    inode_table: Vec<EXT4Inode>,
    block_bitmap: Vec<u8>,
}

#[repr(C)]
pub struct EXT4Superblock {
    pub inodes_count: u32,
    pub blocks_count_lo: u32,
    pub reserved_blocks_count_lo: u32,
    pub free_blocks_count_lo: u32,
    pub free_inodes_count: u32,
    pub first_data_block: u32,
    pub log_block_size: u32,
    pub log_frag_size: u32,
    pub blocks_per_group: u32,
    pub frags_per_group: u32,
    pub inodes_per_group: u32,
    pub mtime: u32,
    pub wtime: u32,
    pub mnt_count: u16,
    pub max_mnt_count: u16,
    pub magic: u16,
    pub state: u16,
    pub errors: u16,
    pub minor_rev_level: u16,
    pub lastcheck: u32,
    pub checkinterval: u32,
    pub creator_os: u32,
    pub rev_level: u32,
    pub def_resuid: u16,
    pub def_resgid: u16,
    pub first_ino: u32,
    pub inode_size: u16,
    pub block_group_nr: u16,
    pub feature_compat: u32,
    pub feature_incompat: u32,
    pub feature_ro_compat: u32,
}

pub struct EXT4Inode {
    pub inode_number: u32,
    pub mode: u16,
    pub uid: u16,
    pub size: u32,
    pub atime: u32,
    pub ctime: u32,
    pub mtime: u32,
    pub dtime: u32, // Deletion time
    pub gid: u16,
    pub links_count: u16,
    pub blocks: u32,
    pub flags: u32,
    pub osd1: u32,
    pub block: [u32; 15],
    pub generation: u32,
    pub file_acl: u32,
    pub dir_acl: u32,
    pub faddr: u32,
    pub osd2: [u8; 12],
}

impl EXT4Parser {
    pub fn new(device: &dyn StorageDevice) -> Result<Self> {
        // Read superblock (typically at offset 1024 bytes)
        let superblock_data = device.read_bytes(1024, 1024)?;
        
        let ptr = superblock_data.as_ptr() 
            as *const EXT4Superblock;
        let superblock = unsafe { ptr.as_ref().unwrap().clone() };
        
        // Validate magic number
        if superblock.magic != 0xEF53 {
            return Err("Invalid EXT4 magic number".into());
        }
        
        Ok(EXT4Parser {
            superblock: superblock.clone(),
            inode_table: Vec::new(),
            block_bitmap: Vec::new(),
        })
    }
    
    pub fn parse_inode_table(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<()> {
        let block_size = 1024u32 << self.superblock.log_block_size;
        let inode_size = self.superblock.inode_size as u32;
        let inodes_per_group = self.superblock.inodes_per_group;
        
        // Read inode table for first group
        // (typically at block 2)
        let inode_table_block = 2;
        let offset = inode_table_block as u64 * block_size as u64;
        
        let num_inodes = std::cmp::min(
            inodes_per_group,
            self.superblock.inodes_count
        );
        
        for i in 0..num_inodes {
            let inode_offset = offset + (i as u64 * inode_size as u64);
            
            match device.read_bytes(inode_offset, inode_size as usize) {
                Ok(data) => {
                    if let Ok(inode) = self.parse_inode(&data, i + 1) {
                        self.inode_table.push(inode);
                    }
                }
                Err(_) => break,
            }
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn parse_inode(&self, data: &[u8], inode_num: u32) 
        -> Result<EXT4Inode> {
        if data.len() < 128 {
            return Err("Inode data too small".into());
        }
        
        let ptr = data.as_ptr() as *const EXT4Inode;
        let mut inode = unsafe { ptr.as_ref().unwrap().clone() };
        inode.inode_number = inode_num;
        
        Ok(inode)
    }
    
    fn parse_directory_entry(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<(String, u32)> {
        let mut entries = Vec::new();
        let mut offset = 0;
        
        while offset < data.len() {
            if offset + 8 > data.len() {
                break;
            }
            
            let inode = u32::from_le_bytes(
                data[offset..offset + 4].try_into().unwrap()
            );
            let entry_len = u16::from_le_bytes(
                data[offset + 4..offset + 6].try_into().unwrap()
            ) as usize;
            let name_len = data[offset + 6] as usize;
            
            if entry_len == 0 || entry_len > data.len() - offset {
                break;
            }
            
            if offset + 8 + name_len <= data.len() {
                let name_bytes = &data[offset + 8..offset + 8 + name_len];
                if let Ok(name) = String::from_utf8(name_bytes.to_vec()) {
                    entries.push((name, inode));
                }
            }
            
            offset += entry_len;
        }
        
        entries
    }
}

impl Clone for EXT4Superblock {
    fn clone(&self) -> Self {
        unsafe { std::ptr::read(self) }
    }
}

impl Clone for EXT4Inode {
    fn clone(&self) -> Self {
        unsafe { std::ptr::read(self) }
    }
}

impl FileSystemParser for EXT4Parser {
    fn fs_type(&self)-> FileSystemType {
        FileSystemType::EXT4
    }
    
    fn parse(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<FSMetadata> {
        self.parse_inode_table(device)?;
        
        let block_size = 1024u32 << self.superblock.log_block_size;
        
        Ok(FSMetadata {
            fs_type: FileSystemType::EXT4,
            total_size: (self.superblock.blocks_count_lo as u64) * (block_size as u64),
            used_size: ((self.superblock.blocks_count_lo 
                - self.superblock.free_blocks_count_lo) as u64) * (block_size as u64),
            free_size: (self.superblock.free_blocks_count_lo as u64) * (block_size as u64),
            block_size,
            creation_time: self.superblock.mtime as u64,
            modification_time: self.superblock.wtime as u64,
        })
    }
    
    fn get_allocation_map(&self) -> AllocationMap {
        AllocationMap {
            allocations: self.block_bitmap.clone(),
            sector_size: 1024 << self.superblock.log_block_size,
        }
    }
    
    fn lookup_file(&self, inode: u64) 
        -> Result<Option<FileMetadata>> {
        if let Some(inode_data) = 
            self.inode_table.iter().find(|i| i.inode_number == inode as u32) {
            Ok(Some(FileMetadata {
                inode,
                name: format!("inode_{}", inode),
                size: inode_data.size as u64,
                created: inode_data.ctime as u64,
                modified: inode_data.mtime as u64,
                accessed: inode_data.atime as u64,
                permissions: inode_data.mode as u32,
                owner_uid: Some(inode_data.uid as u32),
                owner_gid: Some(inode_data.gid as u32),
                is_directory: (inode_data.mode & 0x4000) != 0,
                is_symlink: (inode_data.mode & 0xA000) == 0xA000,
                allocation_blocks: Vec::new(),
            }))
        } else {
            Ok(None)
        }
    }
    
    fn get_deleted_entries(&self) -> Vec<DeletedFileEntry> {
        self.inode_table
            .iter()
            .filter(|inode| inode.dtime != 0) // dtime set = deleted
            .map(|inode| DeletedFileEntry {
                original_name: format!("inode_{}", inode.inode_number),
                original_size: inode.size as u64,
                deletion_time: Some(inode.dtime as u64),
                first_cluster: inode.block[0] as u64,
                metadata: FileMetadata {
                    inode: inode.inode_number as u64,
                    name: format!("inode_{}", inode.inode_number),
                    size: inode.size as u64,
                    created: inode.ctime as u64,
                    modified: inode.mtime as u64,
                    accessed: inode.atime as u64,
                    permissions: inode.mode as u32,
                    owner_uid: Some(inode.uid as u32),
                    owner_gid: Some(inode.gid as u32),
                    is_directory: (inode.mode & 0x4000) != 0,
                    is_symlink: (inode.mode & 0xA000) == 0xA000,
                    allocation_blocks: Vec::new(),
                },
            })
            .collect()
    }
    
    fn get_journal_entries(&self) -> Vec<JournalEntry> {
        Vec::new() // Journal parsing implementation
    }
}
```

### 7.1.3 HFS+ Parser Implementation

```rust
pub struct HFSPlusParser {
    volume_header: HFSPlusVolumeHeader,
    catalog_entries: Vec<CatalogRecord>,
}

#[repr(C)]
pub struct HFSPlusVolumeHeader {
    pub signature: u16, // Should be 0x482B (H+)
    pub version: u16,
    pub attributes: u32,
    pub last_mount_time: u32,
    pub backup_time: u32,
    pub checked_time: u32,
    pub num_files: u32,
    pub num_folders: u32,
    pub block_size: u32,
    pub total_blocks: u32,
    pub free_blocks: u32,
    pub next_alloc_block: u32,
    pub write_count: u32,
    pub encoding_hint: u32,
    pub allocation_file_size: u64,
    pub extent_overflow_file_size: u64,
    pub catalog_file_size: u64,
    pub attributes_file_size: u64,
    pub startup_file_size: u64,
}

pub struct CatalogRecord {
    pub parent_cnid: u32,
    pub record_name: String,
    pub cnid: u32, // Catalog Node ID
    pub flags: u16,
    pub file_mode: u32,
    pub file_size: u64,
    pub created_date: u32,
    pub modified_date: u32,
    pub accessed_date: u32,
}

impl HFSPlusParser {
    pub fn new(device: &dyn StorageDevice) -> Result<Self> {
        // Read volume header (at sector 2, offset 1024 bytes)
        let header_data = device.read_bytes(1024, 512)?;
        
        let ptr = header_data.as_ptr() 
            as *const HFSPlusVolumeHeader;
        let header = unsafe { ptr.as_ref().unwrap().clone() };
        
        // Validate signature
        if header.signature != 0x482B {
            return Err("Invalid HFS+ signature".into());
        }
        
        Ok(HFSPlusParser {
            volume_header: header,
            catalog_entries: Vec::new(),
        })
    }
    
    pub fn parse_catalog(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<()> {
        // Catalog file is located in extents
        // Typically after allocation bitmap
        
        let catalog_start = 16 * self.volume_header.block_size as u64;
        let catalog_size = self.volume_header.catalog_file_size as usize;
        
        match device.read_bytes(catalog_start, catalog_size) {
            Ok(data) => {
                self.parse_btree_catalog(&data);
            }
            Err(_) => return Err("Failed to read catalog".into()),
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn parse_btree_catalog(&mut self, data: &[u8]) {
        // B-tree parsing for HFS+ catalog
        // Structure: header, index nodes, leaf nodes
        
        if data.len() < 512 {
            return;
        }
        
        // Parse B-tree header
        let _node_size = u16::from_be_bytes(
            data[32..34].try_into().unwrap_or([0; 2])
        );
        let _num_nodes = u32::from_be_bytes(
            data[36..40].try_into().unwrap_or([0; 4])
        );
        let _num_free_nodes = u32::from_be_bytes(
            data[40..44].try_into().unwrap_or([0; 4])
        );
        
        // Parse leaf nodes (catalog records)
        // This is simplified - full implementation would traverse tree
        let mut offset = 512; // Skip header
        
        while offset < data.len() {
            if offset + 14 > data.len() {
                break;
            }
            
            // Simple record parsing
            let _parent_cnid = u32::from_be_bytes(
                data[offset..offset + 4].try_into().unwrap_or([0; 4])
            );
            let name_len = data[offset + 6] as usize;
            
            if offset + 8 + name_len > data.len() {
                break;
            }
            
            let name_bytes = &data[offset + 8..offset + 8 + name_len];
            if let Ok(name) = String::from_utf8(name_bytes.to_vec()) {
                self.catalog_entries.push(CatalogRecord {
                    parent_cnid: _parent_cnid,
                    record_name: name,
                    cnid: 0,
                    flags: 0,
                    file_mode: 0o644,
                    file_size: 0,
                    created_date: 0,
                    modified_date: 0,
                    accessed_date: 0,
                });
            }
            
            offset += 14 + name_len;
        }
    }
}

impl Clone for HFSPlusVolumeHeader {
    fn clone(&self) -> Self {
        unsafe { std::ptr::read(self) }
    }
}

impl FileSystemParser for HFSPlusParser {
    fn fs_type(&self) -> FileSystemType {
        FileSystemType::HFSPlus
    }
    
    fn parse(&mut self, device: &dyn StorageDevice) 
        -> Result<FSMetadata> {
        self.parse_catalog(device)?;
        
        Ok(FSMetadata {
            fs_type: FileSystemType::HFSPlus,
            total_size: (self.volume_header.total_blocks as u64) 
                * (self.volume_header.block_size as u64),
            used_size: ((self.volume_header.total_blocks 
                - self.volume_header.free_blocks) as u64) 
                * (self.volume_header.block_size as u64),
            free_size: (self.volume_header.free_blocks as u64) 
                * (self.volume_header.block_size as u64),
            block_size: self.volume_header.block_size,
            creation_time: self.volume_header.last_mount_time as u64,
            modification_time: self.volume_header.backup_time as u64,
        })
    }
    
    fn get_allocation_map(&self) -> AllocationMap {
        AllocationMap {
            allocations: Vec::new(),
            sector_size: self.volume_header.block_size as usize,
        }
    }
    
    fn lookup_file(&self, inode: u64) 
        -> Result<Option<FileMetadata>> {
        if let Some(record) = 
            self.catalog_entries.iter().find(|r| r.cnid as u64 == inode) {
            Ok(Some(FileMetadata {
                inode,
                name: record.record_name.clone(),
                size: record.file_size,
                created: record.created_date as u64,
                modified: record.modified_date as u64,
                accessed: record.accessed_date as u64,
                permissions: record.file_mode,
                owner_uid: None,
                owner_gid: None,
                is_directory: (record.flags & 0x10) != 0,
                is_symlink: (record.flags & 0x20) != 0,
                allocation_blocks: Vec::new(),
            }))
        } else {
            Ok(None)
        }
    }
    
    fn get_deleted_entries(&self) -> Vec<DeletedFileEntry> {
        // HFS+ doesn't easily track deleted entries
        // Requires journal parsing or special tools
        Vec::new()
    }
    
    fn get_journal_entries(&self) -> Vec<JournalEntry> {
        // Parse HFS+ journal
        Vec::new()
    }
}
```

## 8. SCAN ENGINE ARCHITECTURE & IMPLEMENTATION

### 8.1 Core Scan Engine Components

```rust
pub struct ScanEngine {
    device: Arc<dyn StorageDevice>,
    sector_reader: Arc<SectorReader>,
    signature_detector: Arc<SignatureDetector>,
    clustering_engine: Arc<ClusteringEngine>,
    fs_parser_manager: Arc<FileSystemParserManager>,
    event_dispatcher: Arc<EventDispatcher>,
    cache: Arc<ScanCache>,
    stats: Arc<parking_lot::RwLock<ScanStats>>,
}

pub struct ScanStats {
    pub sectors_scanned: u64,
    pub files_found: u32,
    pub bytes_processed: u64,
    pub start_time: std::time::Instant,
    pub last_update: std::time::Instant,
    pub current_speed_mbps: f32,
}

impl ScanEngine {
    pub fn new(
        device: Arc<dyn StorageDevice>,
        event_dispatcher: Arc<EventDispatcher>,
    ) -> Self {
        ScanEngine {
            device,
            sector_reader: Arc::new(SectorReader::new()),
            signature_detector: Arc::new(SignatureDetector::new()),
            clustering_engine: Arc::new(ClusteringEngine::new()),
            fs_parser_manager: Arc::new(FileSystemParserManager::new()),
            event_dispatcher,
            cache: Arc::new(ScanCache::new()),
            stats: Arc::new(parking_lot::RwLock::new(ScanStats {
                sectors_scanned: 0,
                files_found: 0,
                bytes_processed: 0,
                start_time: std::time::Instant::now(),
                last_update: std::time::Instant::now(),
                current_speed_mbps: 0.0,
            })),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn scan(
        &self,
        config: ScanConfig,
    ) -> Result<Vec<FileMeta>> {
        self.event_dispatcher.dispatch(Event::ScanStarted {
            device: self.device.device_id(),
        });
        
        // Phase 1: Detect file system
        let fs_type = self.detect_filesystem().await?;
        
        // Phase 2: Read and analyze sectors
        let candidates = self.scan_sectors(&config).await?;
        
        // Phase 3: Cluster fragmented files
        let clustered = self.clustering_engine
            .cluster_candidates(candidates)
            .await?;
        
        // Phase 4: Validate with file system metadata
        let validated = self.validate_with_filesystem(
            clustered,
            &fs_type,
        ).await?;
        
        // Phase 5: Generate final results
        let results = self.finalize_results(validated).await?;
        
        self.event_dispatcher.dispatch(Event::ScanCompleted {
            files_found: results.len(),
            duration_ms: self.stats.read().start_time.elapsed().as_millis() as u64,
        });
        
        Ok(results)
    }
    
    async fn detect_filesystem(&self) 
        -> Result<FileSystemType> {
        // Read boot sector and identify file system
        let boot_data = self.device.read_sectors(0, 1)?;
        
        // Check for NTFS
        if boot_data.len() > 11 && &boot_data[3..11] == b"NTFS    " {
            return Ok(FileSystemType::NTFS);
        }
        
        // Check for HFS+
        let sig_offset = 1024usize;
        if boot_data.len() > sig_offset + 2 {
            let sig = u16::from_be_bytes(
                boot_data[sig_offset..sig_offset + 2]
                    .try_into()
                    .unwrap_or([0; 2])
            );
            if sig == 0x482B {
                return Ok(FileSystemType::HFSPlus);
            }
        }
        
        // Check for EXT4 (superblock at offset 1024)
        if boot_data.len() > 1026 {
            let sig = u16::from_le_bytes(
                boot_data[1024 + 56..1024 + 58]
                    .try_into()
                    .unwrap_or([0; 2])
            );
            if sig == 0xEF53 {
                return Ok(FileSystemType::EXT4);
            }
        }
        
        Ok(FileSystemType::Unknown)
    }
    
    async fn scan_sectors(&self, config: &ScanConfig) 
        -> Result<Vec<FileCandidate>> {
        let total_sectors = self.device.get_total_sectors();
        let sector_size = self.device.get_sector_size();
        let mut candidates = Vec::new();
        
        // Determine read strategy
        let read_ahead = match config.scan_type {
            ScanType::Quick => 256,      // 256 sectors
            ScanType::Normal => 512,
            ScanType::Deep => 1024,
        };
        
        let chunk_size = read_ahead * sector_size;
        
        // Progress tracking
        let mut processed_sectors = 0u64;
        
        // Scan in chunks
        for chunk_start in (0..total_sectors).step_by(read_ahead as usize) {
            let chunk_end = std::cmp::min(
                chunk_start + read_ahead as u64,
                total_sectors
            );
            let num_sectors = chunk_end - chunk_start;
            
            // Read chunk
            let data = self.device.read_sectors(chunk_start, num_sectors)?;
            
            // Detect signatures in parallel
            let chunk_candidates: Vec<_> = (0..data.len())
                .into_par_iter()
                .step_by(1)
                .filter_map(|offset| {
                    self.signature_detector
                        .detect_at_offset(&data, offset)
                        .map(|sig| FileCandidate {
                            sector_offset: chunk_start as u64 
                                + (offset / sector_size) as u64,
                            signature: sig,
                            confidence: 0.95,
                        })
                })
                .collect();
            
            candidates.extend(chunk_candidates);
            processed_sectors += num_sectors;
            
            // Update progress
            let progress = (processed_sectors as f32 / total_sectors as f32) * 100.0;
            self.event_dispatcher.dispatch(Event::ProgressUpdate {
                progress,
                files_found: candidates.len() as u32,
            });
            
            // Update stats
            let mut stats = self.stats.write();
            stats.sectors_scanned = processed_sectors;
            stats.bytes_processed = processed_sectors * sector_size as u64;
            stats.files_found = candidates.len() as u32;
        }
        
        Ok(candidates)
    }
    
    async fn validate_with_filesystem(
        &self,
        candidates: Vec<FileCandidate>,
        fs_type: &FileSystemType,
    ) -> Result<Vec<FileMeta>> {
        let mut validated = Vec::new();
        
        // Parse file system metadata
        let mut parser = self.fs_parser_manager
            .create_parser(fs_type)?;
        parser.parse(&*self.device)?;
        
        // Cross-reference with file system
        for candidate in candidates {
            let mut file_meta = FileMeta {
                signature: candidate.signature.clone(),
                first_sector: candidate.sector_offset,
                last_verified_sector: candidate.sector_offset,
                estimated_size: candidate.signature.typical_size,
                recovery_confidence: candidate.confidence,
                file_type: candidate.signature.file_type.clone(),
                fragments: vec![],
            };
            
            // Increase confidence if found in FS metadata
            let allocation_map = parser.get_allocation_map();
            let sector_allocated = candidate.sector_offset as usize 
                < allocation_map.allocations.len() 
                && allocation_map.allocations[candidate.sector_offset as usize];
            
            if sector_allocated {
                file_meta.recovery_confidence = 0.98;
            }
            
            validated.push(file_meta);
        }
        
        Ok(validated)
    }
    
    async fn finalize_results(&self, mut validated: Vec<FileMeta>) 
        -> Result<Vec<FileMeta>> {
        // Deduplicate overlapping files
        validated.sort_by_key(|f| f.first_sector);
        
        let mut final_results = Vec::new();
        let mut last_sector = 0u64;
        
        for file in validated {
            // Skip if completely overlaps previous
            if file.first_sector < last_sector {
                continue;
            }
            
            last_sector = file.last_verified_sector;
            final_results.push(file);
        }
        
        Ok(final_results)
    }
}

pub struct FileCandidate {
    pub sector_offset: u64,
    pub signature: FileSignature,
    pub confidence: f32,
}

pub struct FileMeta {
    pub signature: FileSignature,
    pub first_sector: u64,
    pub last_verified_sector: u64,
    pub estimated_size: u64,
    pub recovery_confidence: f32,
    pub file_type: String,
    pub fragments: Vec<SectorRange>,
}

pub struct SectorRange {
    pub start: u64,
    pub end: u64,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ScanConfig {
    pub scan_type: ScanType,
    pub skip_system_files: bool,
    pub min_file_size: u64,
    pub max_file_size: u64,
    pub target_file_types: Option<Vec<String>>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum ScanType {
    Quick,
    Normal,
    Deep,
}
```

### 8.2 Sector Reader Implementation

```rust
pub struct SectorReader {
    buffer_pool: Arc<BufferPool>,
}

pub struct BufferPool {
    buffers: Vec<Vec<u8>>,
}

impl SectorReader {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        SectorReader {
            buffer_pool: Arc::new(BufferPool::new(16, 1024 * 1024)), // 16 x 1MB buffers
        }
    }
    
    pub fn read_ahead(
        &self,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
        start_sector: u64,
        num_sectors: u64,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
        let sector_size = device.get_sector_size();
        let total_bytes = (num_sectors * sector_size as u64) as usize;
        
        // Get buffer from pool
        let mut buffer = self.buffer_pool.acquire(total_bytes);
        
        // Read data
        let data = device.read_sectors(start_sector, num_sectors)?;
        buffer.extend_from_slice(&data);
        
        Ok(buffer)
    }
}

impl BufferPool {
    pub fn new(num_buffers: usize, buffer_size: usize) -> Self {
        BufferPool {
            buffers: vec![Vec::with_capacity(buffer_size); num_buffers],
        }
    }
    
    pub fn acquire(&self, required_size: usize) -> Vec<u8> {
        // Get pre-allocated buffer or create new
        Vec::with_capacity(required_size)
    }
}
```

### 8.3 Signature Detection Engine

```rust
pub struct SignatureDetector {
    signatures: Arc<Vec<FileSignature>>,
    compiled_patterns: Arc<Vec<CompiledPattern>>,
}

pub struct FileSignature {
    pub file_type: String,
    pub magic_bytes: Vec<u8>,
    pub pattern: String,
    pub typical_size: u64,
    pub min_size: u64,
    pub max_size: u64,
    pub footer_bytes: Option<Vec<u8>>,
    pub confidence_base: f32,
}

pub struct CompiledPattern {
    pub signature: FileSignature,
    pub automaton: Option<String>, // Aho-Corasick or similar
}

impl SignatureDetector {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        let signatures = Arc::new(Self::load_signatures());
        let compiled_patterns = Arc::new(
            signatures.iter()
                .map(|sig| CompiledPattern {
                    signature: sig.clone(),
                    automaton: None,
                })
                .collect()
        );
        
        SignatureDetector {
            signatures,
            compiled_patterns,
        }
    }
    
    pub fn detect_at_offset(
        &self,
        buffer: &[u8],
        offset: usize,
    ) -> Option<FileSignature> {
        for sig in self.signatures.iter() {
            if offset + sig.magic_bytes.len() > buffer.len() {
                continue;
            }
            
            // Check magic bytes
            if &buffer[offset..offset + sig.magic_bytes.len()] 
                == sig.magic_bytes.as_slice() {
                return Some(sig.clone());
            }
        }
        None
    }
    
    fn load_signatures() -> Vec<FileSignature> {
        vec![
            // JPEG
            FileSignature {
                file_type: "JPEG".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![0xFF, 0xD8, 0xFF],
                pattern: "JPEG image".to_string(),
                typical_size: 2_000_000,
                min_size: 1000,
                max_size: 500_000_000,
                footer_bytes: Some(vec![0xFF, 0xD9]),
                confidence_base: 0.95,
            },
            
            // PNG
            FileSignature {
                file_type: "PNG".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![0x89, 0x50, 0x4E, 0x47],
                pattern: "PNG image".to_string(),
                typical_size: 1_000_000,
                min_size: 1000,
                max_size: 1_000_000_000,
                footer_bytes: Some(vec![0x49, 0x45, 0x4E, 0x44]),
                confidence_base: 0.98,
            },
            
            // PDF
            FileSignature {
                file_type: "PDF".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![0x25, 0x50, 0x44, 0x46], // %PDF
                pattern: "PDF document".to_string(),
                typical_size: 1_000_000,
                min_size: 1000,
                max_size: 2_000_000_000,
                footer_bytes: Some(vec![0x25, 0x25, 0x45, 0x4F, 0x46]), // %%EOF
                confidence_base: 0.96,
            },
            
            // ZIP/Office
            FileSignature {
                file_type: "ZIP".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![0x50, 0x4B, 0x03, 0x04], // PK..
                pattern: "ZIP archive".to_string(),
                typical_size: 5_000_000,
                min_size: 1000,
                max_size: 5_000_000_000,
                footer_bytes: Some(vec![0x50, 0x4B, 0x05, 0x06]),
                confidence_base: 0.92,
            },
            
            // MP4 Video
            FileSignature {
                file_type: "MP4".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x20, 0x66, 0x74, 0x79, 0x70],
                pattern: "MP4 video".to_string(),
                typical_size: 50_000_000,
                min_size: 10000,
                max_size: 10_000_000_000,
                footer_bytes: None,
                confidence_base: 0.94,
            },
            
            // GIF
            FileSignature {
                file_type: "GIF".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![0x47, 0x49, 0x46], // GIF
                pattern: "GIF image".to_string(),
                typical_size: 500_000,
                min_size: 1000,
                max_size: 100_000_000,
                footer_bytes: Some(vec![0x00, 0x3B]),
                confidence_base: 0.93,
            },
        ]
    }
    
    pub fn detect_in_buffer(&self, buffer: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<FileCandidate> {
        let mut candidates = Vec::new();
        
        for (offset, _) in buffer.iter().enumerate() {
            if let Some(sig) = self.detect_at_offset(buffer, offset) {
                candidates.push(FileCandidate {
                    sector_offset: (offset / 4096) as u64,
                    signature: sig,
                    confidence: 0.90,
                });
            }
        }
        
        candidates
    }
}

impl Clone for FileSignature {
    fn clone(&self) -> Self {
        FileSignature {
            file_type: self.file_type.clone(),
            magic_bytes: self.magic_bytes.clone(),
            pattern: self.pattern.clone(),
            typical_size: self.typical_size,
            min_size: self.min_size,
            max_size: self.max_size,
            footer_bytes: self.footer_bytes.clone(),
            confidence_base: self.confidence_base,
        }
    }
}
```

## 9. RECOVERY ENGINE TECHNICAL SPECIFICATIONS

### 9.1 Recovery Engine Core

```rust
pub struct RecoveryEngine {
    device: Arc<dyn StorageDevice>,
    sector_reader: Arc<SectorReader>,
    strategies: Vec<Box<dyn RecoveryStrategy>>,
    event_dispatcher: Arc<EventDispatcher>,
    integrity_checker: Arc<IntegrityChecker>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
pub trait RecoveryStrategy: Send + Sync {
    fn name(&self) -> &str;
    fn can_recover(&self, file_meta: &FileMeta) -> bool;
    fn priority(&self) -> u32; // Higher = better
    
    async fn recover(
        &self,
        file_meta: &FileMeta,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>>;
    
    fn confidence_score(&self) -> f32;
}

/// Strategy 1: Metadata-based recovery
pub struct MetadataBasedStrategy {
    fs_metadata: Arc<FileSystemMetadata>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl RecoveryStrategy for MetadataBasedStrategy {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "Metadata-Based Recovery"
    }
    
    fn can_recover(&self, file_meta: &FileMeta) -> bool {
        // Can recover if file system has metadata
        !file_meta.fragments.is_empty()
    }
    
    fn priority(&self) -> u32 {
        100 // Highest priority
    }
    
    async fn recover(
        &self,
        file_meta: &FileMeta,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
        let mut recovered_data = Vec::new();
        
        // Follow allocation chain from file system metadata
        for fragment in &file_meta.fragments {
            let data = device.read_sectors(
                fragment.start,
                fragment.end - fragment.start,
            )?;
            recovered_data.extend_from_slice(&data);
        }
        
        // Truncate to actual file size
        recovered_data.truncate(file_meta.estimated_size as usize);
        
        Ok(recovered_data)
    }
    
    fn confidence_score(&self) -> f32 {
        0.98 // Very high confidence
    }
}

/// Strategy 2: Signature-based recovery
pub struct SignatureBasedStrategy {
    signature_detector: Arc<SignatureDetector>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl RecoveryStrategy for SignatureBasedStrategy {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "Signature-Based Recovery"
    }
    
    fn can_recover(&self, file_meta: &FileMeta) -> bool {
        !file_meta.signature.magic_bytes.is_empty()
    }
    
    fn priority(&self) -> u32 {
        70
    }
    
    async fn recover(
        &self,
        file_meta: &FileMeta,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
        let mut recovered_data = Vec::new();
        
        // Start from detected sector
        let start_sector = file_meta.first_sector;
        let estimated_size = file_meta.estimated_size as usize;
        let sector_size = device.get_sector_size();
        
        let sectors_needed = (estimated_size + sector_size - 1) / sector_size;
        
        // Read sectors sequentially
        let data = device.read_sectors(start_sector, sectors_needed as u64)?;
        recovered_data.extend_from_slice(&data);
        
        // Truncate to estimated size
        recovered_data.truncate(estimated_size);
        
        // Look for footer/terminator
        if let Some(footer) = &file_meta.signature.footer_bytes {
            if let Some(pos) = Self::find_footer(&recovered_data, footer) {
                recovered_data.truncate(pos + footer.len());
            }
        }
        
        Ok(recovered_data)
    }
    
    fn confidence_score(&self) -> f32 {
        0.85 // Good confidence
    }
}

impl SignatureBasedStrategy {
    fn find_footer(data: &[u8], footer: &[u8]) -> Option<usize> {
        data.windows(footer.len())
            .position(|window| window == footer)
    }
}

/// Strategy 3: Carving-based recovery
pub struct CarvingStrategy {
    clustering_engine: Arc<ClusteringEngine>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl RecoveryStrategy for CarvingStrategy {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "Carving-Based Recovery"
    }
    
    fn can_recover(&self, _file_meta: &FileMeta) -> bool {
        true // Can always attempt carving
    }
    
    fn priority(&self) -> u32 {
        40 // Lower priority, use as fallback
    }
    
    async fn recover(
        &self,
        file_meta: &FileMeta,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
        // Cluster sectors based on adjacency and patterns
        let clustered_sectors = self.clustering_engine
            .cluster_around_start(file_meta.first_sector)
            .await?;
        
        let mut recovered_data = Vec::new();
        
        // Read clustered sectors in order
        for sector in clustered_sectors {
            let data = device.read_sectors(sector, 1)?;
            recovered_data.extend_from_slice(&data);
        }
        
        recovered_data.truncate(file_meta.estimated_size as usize);
        
        Ok(recovered_data)
    }
    
    fn confidence_score(&self) -> f32 {
        0.75 // Moderate confidence
    }
}

impl RecoveryEngine {
    pub fn new(
        device: Arc<dyn StorageDevice>,
        event_dispatcher: Arc<EventDispatcher>,
    ) -> Self {
        RecoveryEngine {
            device,
            sector_reader: Arc::new(SectorReader::new()),
            strategies: vec![
                Box::new(MetadataBasedStrategy {
                    fs_metadata: Arc::new(FileSystemMetadata::new()),
                }),
                Box::new(SignatureBasedStrategy {
                    signature_detector: Arc::new(SignatureDetector::new()),
                }),
                Box::new(CarvingStrategy {
                    clustering_engine: Arc::new(ClusteringEngine::new()),
                }),
            ],
            event_dispatcher,
            integrity_checker: Arc::new(IntegrityChecker::new()),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn recover_file(
        &self,
        file_meta: &FileMeta,
        destination: &Path,
    ) -> Result<RecoveryResult> {
        self.event_dispatcher.dispatch(Event::RecoveryStarted {
            file_name: file_meta.signature.file_type.clone(),
        });
        
        // Try strategies in priority order
        let mut recovered_data = None;
        let mut used_strategy = String::new();
        let mut confidence_score = 0.0f32;
        
        for strategy in self.strategies.iter() {
            if strategy.can_recover(file_meta) {
                match strategy.recover(file_meta, &*self.device).await {
                    Ok(data) => {
                        recovered_data = Some(data);
                        used_strategy = strategy.name().to_string();
                        confidence_score = strategy.confidence_score();
                        break;
                    }
                    Err(_) => continue,
                }
            }
        }
        
        if recovered_data.is_none() {
            return Err("All recovery strategies failed".into());
        }
        
        let data = recovered_data.unwrap();
        
        // Verify integrity
        let integrity = self.integrity_checker
            .check(&data, file_meta)
            .await?;
        
        // Write to destination
        self.write_file(destination, &data).await?;
        
        let result = RecoveryResult {
            file_name: file_meta.signature.file_type.clone(),
            destination: destination.to_path_buf(),
            data_size: data.len() as u64,
            file_hash: self.calculate_hash(&data),
            integrity_status: integrity,
            recovery_strategy: used_strategy,
            confidence: confidence_score,
            recovery_time_ms: 0,
        };
        
        self.event_dispatcher.dispatch(Event::RecoveryCompleted {
            success: true,
            file: result.clone(),
        });
        
        Ok(result)
    }
    
    async fn write_file(&self, path: &Path, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<()> {
        use tokio::fs;
        
        // Create parent directories
        if let Some(parent) = path.parent() {
            fs::create_dir_all(parent).await?;
        }
        
        // Write to temporary file first
        let temp_path = path.with_extension("tmp");
        fs::write(&temp_path, data).await?;
        
        // Atomic rename
        fs::rename(temp_path, path).await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn calculate_hash(&self, data: &[u8]) -> String {
        use sha2::{Sha256, Digest};
        
        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();
        hasher.update(data);
        let result = hasher.finalize();
        
        format!("{:x}", result)
    }
}

pub struct RecoveryResult {
    pub file_name: String,
    pub destination: PathBuf,
    pub data_size: u64,
    pub file_hash: String,
    pub integrity_status: IntegrityStatus,
    pub recovery_strategy: String,
    pub confidence: f32,
    pub recovery_time_ms: u64,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum IntegrityStatus {
    Perfect,
    Good,
    Fair,
    Poor,
    Corrupted,
}

pub struct IntegrityChecker {
    handlers: Arc<Vec<Box<dyn FileTypeHandler>>>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
pub trait FileTypeHandler: Send + Sync {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str>;
    async fn validate(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<IntegrityStatus>;
}

impl IntegrityChecker {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        IntegrityChecker {
            handlers: Arc::new(vec![
                Box::new(JPEGHandler),
                Box::new(PNGHandler),
                Box::new(PDFHandler),
            ]),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn check(
        &self,
        data: &[u8],
        file_meta: &FileMeta,
    ) -> Result<IntegrityStatus> {
        // Find appropriate handler
        for handler in self.handlers.iter() {
            if handler.supported_types()
                .contains(&file_meta.signature.file_type.as_str()) {
                return handler.validate(data).await;
            }
        }
        
        // Default: basic checks
        if data.len() > 0 && data.len() < 10_000_000_000 {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Good)
        } else {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Fair)
        }
    }
}

pub struct JPEGHandler;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl FileTypeHandler for JPEGHandler {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str> {
        vec!["JPEG"]
    }
    
    async fn validate(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<IntegrityStatus> {
        if data.len() < 4 {
            return Ok(IntegrityStatus::Corrupted);
        }
        
        // Check SOI marker
        if &data[0..2] != &[0xFF, 0xD8] {
            return Ok(IntegrityStatus::Corrupted);
        }
        
        // Check EOI marker
        if data.len() >= 2 && &data[data.len()-2..] == &[0xFF, 0xD9] {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Perfect)
        } else {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Good)
        }
    }
}

pub struct PNGHandler;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl FileTypeHandler for PNGHandler {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str> {
        vec!["PNG"]
    }
    
    async fn validate(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<IntegrityStatus> {
        if data.len() < 8 {
            return Ok(IntegrityStatus::Corrupted);
        }
        
        // Check PNG signature
        if &data[0..8] != b"\x89PNG\r\n\x1a\n" {
            return Ok(IntegrityStatus::Corrupted);
        }
        
        // Check IEND chunk
        if data.len() >= 12 && &data[data.len()-12..data.len()-4] == b"IEND" {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Perfect)
        } else {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Good)
        }
    }
}

pub struct PDFHandler;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl FileTypeHandler for PDFHandler {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str> {
        vec!["PDF"]
    }
    
    async fn validate(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<IntegrityStatus> {
        if data.len() < 4 {
            return Ok(IntegrityStatus::Corrupted);
        }
        
        // Check PDF header
        if !data.starts_with(b"%PDF") {
            return Ok(IntegrityStatus::Corrupted);
        }
        
        // Check for %%EOF
        if data.windows(5).any(|w| w == b"%%EOF") {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Perfect)
        } else {
            Ok(IntegrityStatus::Good)
        }
    }
}
```

## 10. FILE ANALYSIS & CLASSIFICATION SYSTEM

### 10.1 File Analysis Pipeline

```rust
pub struct FileAnalyzer {
    type_detectors: Vec<Arc<dyn TypeDetector>>,
    deduplicator: Arc<Deduplicator>,
    metadata_extractor: Arc<MetadataExtractor>,
    ml_classifier: Arc<MLClassifier>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
pub trait TypeDetector: Send + Sync {
    fn name(&self) -> &str;
    async fn detect(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Option<FileType>>;
    fn confidence(&self) -> f32;
}

pub struct MagicBytesDetector;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl TypeDetector for MagicBytesDetector {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "Magic Bytes Detection"
    }
    
    async fn detect(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Option<FileType>> {
        if data.len() < 4 {
            return Ok(None);
        }
        
        match &data[0..4] {
            b"\xFF\xD8\xFF\xE0" | b"\xFF\xD8\xFF\xE1" => {
                Ok(Some(FileType::JPEG))
            }
            b"\x89PNG" => Ok(Some(FileType::PNG)),
            b"%PDF" => Ok(Some(FileType::PDF)),
            b"PK\x03\x04" => Ok(Some(FileType::ZIP)),
            _ => Ok(None),
        }
    }
    
    fn confidence(&self) -> f32 {
        0.95
    }
}

pub struct ExtensionDetector;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl TypeDetector for ExtensionDetector {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "Extension-Based Detection"
    }
    
    async fn detect(&self, _data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Option<FileType>> {
        // Uses file extension from metadata
        Ok(None)
    }
    
    fn confidence(&self) -> f32 {
        0.70
    }
}

pub struct StructureAnalysisDetector;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl TypeDetector for StructureAnalysisDetector {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "Structure Analysis Detection"
    }
    
    async fn detect(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Option<FileType>> {
        // Deep structural analysis
        
        // Check for ZIP (Office, JAR, etc.)
        if Self::is_zip_structure(data) {
            return Ok(Some(FileType::ZIP));
        }
        
        // Check for ELF binary
        if data.len() > 4 && &data[0..4] == b"\x7FELF" {
            return Ok(Some(FileType::ELF));
        }
        
        Ok(None)
    }
    
    fn confidence(&self) -> f32 {
        0.88
    }
}

impl StructureAnalysisDetector {
    fn is_zip_structure(data: &[u8]) -> bool {
        if data.len() < 30 {
            return false;
        }
        
        // PK header
        if &data[0..4] != b"PK\x03\x04" {
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check for central directory
        let has_central_dir = data.windows(4)
            .any(|w| w == b"PK\x01\x02");
        
        has_central_dir
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum FileType {
    JPEG,
    PNG,
    BMP,
    GIF,
    TIFF,
    PDF,
    DOC,
    DOCX,
    XLS,
    XLSX,
    PPT,
    PPTX,
    ZIP,
    RAR,
    ZIP_7Z,
    MP3,
    MP4,
    AVI,
    WAV,
    EXE,
    DLL,
    ELF,
    MAH,
    Unknown,
}

pub struct Deduplicator {
    hashes: Arc<DashMap<String, Vec<u64>>>,
}

impl Deduplicator {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        Deduplicator {
            hashes: Arc::new(DashMap::new()),
        }
    }
    
    pub fn is_duplicate(&self, hash: &str) -> bool {
        self.hashes.contains_key(hash)
    }
    
    pub fn register(&self, hash: String, file_id: u64) {
        self.hashes
            .entry(hash)
            .or_insert_with(Vec::new)
            .push(file_id);
    }
}

pub struct MetadataExtractor;

impl MetadataExtractor {
    pub fn extract_jpeg(data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Option<JpegMetadata>> {
        if data.len() < 20 {
            return Ok(None);
        }
        
        // Parse EXIF data (simplified)
        // Full implementation would parse APP1 marker
        
        Ok(Some(JpegMetadata {
            width: None,
            height: None,
            exif_data: None,
            datetime: None,
        }))
    }
    
    pub fn extract_pdf(data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Option<PdfMetadata>> {
        // Parse PDF document info
        let title = Self::extract_pdf_string(data, "/Title");
        let author = Self::extract_pdf_string(data, "/Author");
        let created = Self::extract_pdf_string(data, "/CreationDate");
        
        Ok(Some(PdfMetadata {
            title,
            author,
            creation_date: created,
            page_count: None,
        }))
    }
    
    fn extract_pdf_string(data: &[u8], key: &str) 
        -> Option<String> {
        let key_bytes = key.as_bytes();
        
        data.windows(key_bytes.len())
            .position(|w| w == key_bytes)
            .and_then(|pos| {
                let start = pos + key_bytes.len();
                if start + 20 >= data.len() {
                    return None;
                }
                
                // Look for parentheses
                data[start..start + 200]
                    .windows(1)
                    .position(|w| w == b"(")
                    .and_then(|paren_pos| {
                        let end = start + paren_pos + 200;
                        data[start + paren_pos..end]
                            .windows(1)
                            .position(|w| w == b")")
                            .map(|close_pos| {
                                let val_start = start + paren_pos + 1;
                                let val_end = val_start + close_pos;
                                String::from_utf8_lossy(
                                    &data[val_start..val_end]
                                ).to_string()
                            })
                    })
            })
    }
}

pub struct JpegMetadata {
    pub width: Option<u32>,
    pub height: Option<u32>,
    pub exif_data: Option<String>,
    pub datetime: Option<String>,
}

pub struct PdfMetadata {
    pub title: Option<String>,
    pub author: Option<String>,
    pub creation_date: Option<String>,
    pub page_count: Option<u32>,
}

pub struct MLClassifier {
    model: Arc<tch::nn::Sequential>,
}

impl MLClassifier {
    pub fn new() -> Result<Self> {
        // Load pre-trained model
        let vs = tch::nn::VarStore::new(tch::Device::Cpu);
        let model = tch::nn::seq(&vs.root(), |p| {
            p.func_res(|p| {
                let seq = tch::nn::seq(p, |p| {
                    tch::nn::linear(p, 256, 128, Default::default());
                    tch::nn::linear(p, 128, 64, Default::default());
                    tch::nn::linear(p, 64, 32, Default::default());
                });
                
                Ok(seq)
            })
        })?;
        
        Ok(MLClassifier {
            model: Arc::new(model),
        })
    }
    
    pub fn classify(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<(FileType, f32)> {
        // Extract features from data
        let features = Self::extract_features(data);
        
        // Run through neural network
        // This is a placeholder - actual implementation would:
        // 1. Convert bytes to feature vector
        // 2. Run through model
        // 3. Get predictions
        
        Ok((FileType::Unknown, 0.5))
    }
    
    fn extract_features(data: &[u8]) -> Vec<f32> {
        let mut features = vec![0.0f32; 256];
        
        // Byte distribution analysis
        for (i, &byte) in data.iter().take(1024).enumerate() {
            features[byte as usize] += 1.0;
        }
        
        // Normalize
        let sum: f32 = features.iter().sum();
        if sum > 0.0 {
            for f in &mut features {
                *f /= sum;
            }
        }
        
        features
    }
}

impl FileAnalyzer {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        FileAnalyzer {
            type_detectors: vec![
                Arc::new(MagicBytesDetector) as Arc<dyn TypeDetector>,
                Arc::new(StructureAnalysisDetector),
                Arc::new(ExtensionDetector),
            ],
            deduplicator: Arc::new(Deduplicator::new()),
            metadata_extractor: Arc::new(MetadataExtractor),
            ml_classifier: Arc::new(MLClassifier::new().unwrap_or_else(|_| {
                MLClassifier {
                    model: Arc::new(unsafe {
                        std::mem::zeroed()
                    }),
                }
            })),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn analyze(&self, data: &[u8], file_id: u64) 
        -> Result<FileAnalysisResult> {
        // Multi-stage detection
        let mut detected_type = FileType::Unknown;
        let mut detection_confidence = 0.0f32;
        
        for detector in &self.type_detectors {
            if let Ok(Some(file_type)) = detector.detect(data).await {
                detected_type = file_type;
                detection_confidence = detector.confidence();
                break;
            }
        }
        
        // Calculate hash for deduplication
        let hash = Self::calculate_hash(data);
        let is_duplicate = self.deduplicator.is_duplicate(&hash);
        
        if !is_duplicate {
            self.deduplicator.register(hash.clone(), file_id);
        }
        
        // Extract metadata
        let metadata = match detected_type {
            FileType::JPEG => {
                MetadataExtractor::extract_jpeg(data)?
                    .map(|m| FileMetadata::Jpeg(m))
            }
            FileType::PDF => {
                MetadataExtractor::extract_pdf(data)?
                    .map(|m| FileMetadata::Pdf(m))
            }
            _ => None,
        };
        
        Ok(FileAnalysisResult {
            detected_type,
            detection_confidence,
            file_hash: hash,
            is_duplicate,
            file_size: data.len() as u64,
            metadata,
        })
    }
    
    fn calculate_hash(data: &[u8]) -> String {
        use std::collections::hash_map::DefaultHasher;
        use std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};
        
        let mut hasher = DefaultHasher::new();
        data.hash(&mut hasher);
        format!("{:x}", hasher.finish())
    }
}

pub struct FileAnalysisResult {
    pub detected_type: FileType,
    pub detection_confidence: f32,
    pub file_hash: String,
    pub is_duplicate: bool,
    pub file_size: u64,
    pub metadata: Option<FileMetadata>,
}

pub enum FileMetadata {
    Jpeg(JpegMetadata),
    Pdf(PdfMetadata),
}
```

## 11. CLUSTERING & REASSEMBLY ALGORITHMS

### 11.1 File Clustering Engine

```rust
pub struct ClusteringEngine {
    sector_graph: Arc<parking_lot::RwLock<SectorGraph>>,
}

pub struct SectorGraph {
    nodes: Vec<SectorNode>,
    edges: Vec<SectorEdge>,
}

pub struct SectorNode {
    sector_id: u64,
    signature: Option<FileSignature>,
    entropy: f32,
    file_type_score: f32,
}

pub struct SectorEdge {
    from: u64,
    to: u64,
    confidence: f32,
    reason: EdgeReason,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum EdgeReason {
    Adjacency,
    SignatureConsistency,
    EntropyPattern,
    FileSystemHint,
    ContentPattern,
}

impl ClusteringEngine {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        ClusteringEngine {
            sector_graph: Arc::new(parking_lot::RwLock::new(
                SectorGraph {
                    nodes: Vec::new(),
                    edges: Vec::new(),
                }
            )),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn cluster_candidates(
        &self,
        candidates: Vec<FileCandidate>,
    ) -> Result<Vec<FileMeta>> {
        let mut clusters = Vec::new();
        let mut processed = std::collections::HashSet::new();
        
        // Sort by sector offset
        let mut sorted_candidates = candidates;
        sorted_candidates.sort_by_key(|c| c.sector_offset);
        
        for candidate in sorted_candidates {
            if processed.contains(&candidate.sector_offset) {
                continue;
            }
            
            // Find connected component
            let cluster = self.bfs_cluster(
                candidate.sector_offset,
                &sorted_candidates,
            ).await?;
            
            if !cluster.is_empty() {
                for sec in &cluster {
                    processed.insert(*sec);
                }
                
                clusters.push(self.build_file_meta(cluster));
            }
        }
        
        Ok(clusters)
    }
    
    async fn bfs_cluster(
        &self,
        start_sector: u64,
        candidates: &[FileCandidate],
    ) -> Result<Vec<u64>> {
        use std::collections::VecDeque;
        
        let mut cluster = Vec::new();
        let mut queue = VecDeque::new();
        let mut visited = std::collections::HashSet::new();
        
        queue.push_back(start_sector);
        visited.insert(start_sector);
        
        while let Some(sector) = queue.pop_front() {
            cluster.push(sector);
            
            // Find adjacent sectors
            for candidate in candidates {
                if !visited.contains(&candidate.sector_offset) {
                    let distance = 
                        (candidate.sector_offset as i64 
                        - sector as i64).abs() as u64;
                    
                    // Within 100 sectors and same file type
                    if distance <= 100 
                        && candidate.signature.file_type 
                        == candidates[0].signature.file_type {
                        queue.push_back(candidate.sector_offset);
                        visited.insert(candidate.sector_offset);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        cluster.sort_unstable();
        Ok(cluster)
    }
    
    fn build_file_meta(&self, sectors: Vec<u64>) 
        -> FileMeta {
        let sector_size = 4096usize; // Default
        let first = sectors[0];
        let last = sectors[sectors.len() - 1];
        
        FileMeta {
            signature: FileSignature {
                file_type: "Unknown".to_string(),
                magic_bytes: vec![],
                pattern: "".to_string(),
                typical_size: (last - first + 1) * sector_size as u64,
                min_size: 0,
                max_size: u64::MAX,
                footer_bytes: None,
                confidence_base: 0.8,
            },
            first_sector: first,
            last_verified_sector: last,
            estimated_size: (last - first + 1) * sector_size as u64,
            recovery_confidence: 0.85,
            file_type: "Unknown".to_string(),
            fragments: vec![
                SectorRange {
                    start: first,
                    end: last + 1,
                }
            ],
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn cluster_around_start(
        &self,
        start_sector: u64,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u64>> {
        Ok(vec![start_sector])
    }
}
```
