# SECTION III: ADVANCED ALGORITHM SPECIFICATIONS

## 12. SECTOR READING & ANALYSIS ALGORITHMS

### 12.1 Advanced Sector Reading Strategy

```rust
pub struct AdvancedSectorReader {
    device: Arc<dyn StorageDevice>,
    cache: Arc<SectorCache>,
    scheduler: Arc<IOScheduler>,
    error_handler: Arc<ErrorRecoveryStrategy>,
}

pub struct SectorCache {
    lru_cache: parking_lot::RwLock<lru::LruCache<u64, Vec<u8>>>,
    hit_count: AtomicU64,
    miss_count: AtomicU64,
}

impl SectorCache {
    pub fn new(capacity: usize) -> Self {
        SectorCache {
            lru_cache: parking_lot::RwLock::new(
                lru::LruCache::new(
                    std::num::NonZeroUsize::new(capacity).unwrap()
                )
            ),
            hit_count: AtomicU64::new(0),
            miss_count: AtomicU64::new(0),
        }
    }
    
    pub fn get(&self, sector: u64) -> Option<Vec<u8>> {
        let mut cache = self.lru_cache.write();
        if let Some(data) = cache.get_mut(&sector) {
            self.hit_count.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
            return Some(data.clone());
        }
        
        self.miss_count.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
        None
    }
    
    pub fn put(&self, sector: u64, data: Vec<u8>) {
        let mut cache = self.lru_cache.write();
        cache.put(sector, data);
    }
    
    pub fn hit_rate(&self) -> f32 {
        let hits = self.hit_count.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
        let misses = self.miss_count.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
        let total = hits + misses;
        
        if total == 0 {
            0.0
        } else {
            hits as f32 / total as f32
        }
    }
}

pub struct IOScheduler {
    queue: Arc<parking_lot::Mutex<std::collections::VecDeque<IORequest>>>,
    algorithm: SchedulingAlgorithm,
}

#[derive(Clone, Copy)]
pub enum SchedulingAlgorithm {
    FCFS,           // First Come First Served
    SSTF,           // Shortest Seek Time First
    SCAN,           // Elevator algorithm
    CSCAN,          // Circular SCAN
    LOOK,           // LOOK algorithm
    CLOOK,          // Circular LOOK
}

pub struct IORequest {
    pub sector: u64,
    pub num_sectors: u64,
    pub priority: u32,
    pub timestamp: std::time::Instant,
}

impl IOScheduler {
    pub fn new(algorithm: SchedulingAlgorithm) -> Self {
        IOScheduler {
            queue: Arc::new(parking_lot::Mutex::new(
                std::collections::VecDeque::new()
            )),
            algorithm,
        }
    }
    
    pub fn schedule(&self, request: IORequest) {
        let mut queue = self.queue.lock();
        
        match self.algorithm {
            SchedulingAlgorithm::FCFS => {
                // Just append to queue
                queue.push_back(request);
            }
            SchedulingAlgorithm::SSTF => {
                // Insert in position with shortest seek time
                let insert_pos = queue
                    .iter()
                    .enumerate()
                    .min_by_key(|(_, r)| {
                        (request.sector as i64 - r.sector as i64).abs()
                    })
                    .map(|(i, _)| i)
                    .unwrap_or(queue.len());
                
                queue.insert(insert_pos, request);
            }
            SchedulingAlgorithm::SCAN => {
                // Sort in direction of head movement
                queue.push_back(request);
                let mut vec: Vec<_> = queue.drain(..).collect();
                vec.sort_by_key(|r| r.sector);
                queue.extend(vec);
            }
            _ => {
                queue.push_back(request);
            }
        }
    }
    
    pub fn next_request(&self) -> Option<IORequest> {
        let mut queue = self.queue.lock();
        queue.pop_front()
    }
    
    pub fn queue_length(&self) -> usize {
        self.queue.lock().len()
    }
}

pub struct ErrorRecoveryStrategy {
    retry_config: RetryConfig,
}

pub struct RetryConfig {
    pub max_retries: u32,
    pub initial_delay_ms: u64,
    pub backoff_multiplier: f32,
    pub max_delay_ms: u64,
}

impl ErrorRecoveryStrategy {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        ErrorRecoveryStrategy {
            retry_config: RetryConfig {
                max_retries: 5,
                initial_delay_ms: 10,
                backoff_multiplier: 2.0,
                max_delay_ms: 1000,
            }
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn read_with_recovery(
        &self,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
        sector: u64,
        num_sectors: u64,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
        let mut current_delay = self.retry_config.initial_delay_ms;
        
        for attempt in 0..=self.retry_config.max_retries {
            match device.read_sectors(sector, num_sectors) {
                Ok(data) => {
                    if attempt > 0 {
                        eprintln!(
                            "Read recovered after {} attempts",
                            attempt
                        );
                    }
                    return Ok(data);
                }
                Err(e) if attempt < self.retry_config.max_retries => {
                    eprintln!(
                        "Read error at sector {} (attempt {}): {}",
                        sector, attempt + 1, e
                    );
                    
                    tokio::time::sleep(
                        tokio::time::Duration::from_millis(
                            current_delay
                        )
                    ).await;
                    
                    current_delay = std::cmp::min(
                        (current_delay as f32 
                            * self.retry_config.backoff_multiplier) as u64,
                        self.retry_config.max_delay_ms,
                    );
                }
                Err(e) => {
                    return Err(format!(
                        "Failed after {} retries: {}",
                        self.retry_config.max_retries, e
                    ).into());
                }
            }
        }
        
        Err("Read failed".into())
    }
}

impl AdvancedSectorReader {
    pub fn new(device: Arc<dyn StorageDevice>) -> Self {
        AdvancedSectorReader {
            device,
            cache: Arc::new(SectorCache::new(1000)),
            scheduler: Arc::new(IOScheduler::new(SchedulingAlgorithm::CLOOK)),
            error_handler: Arc::new(ErrorRecoveryStrategy::new()),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn read_sectors_optimized(
        &self,
        sector: u64,
        num_sectors: u64,
    ) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
        // Check cache first
        if num_sectors == 1 {
            if let Some(cached) = self.cache.get(sector) {
                return Ok(cached);
            }
        }
        
        // Schedule I/O operation
        let request = IORequest {
            sector,
            num_sectors,
            priority: 50,
            timestamp: std::time::Instant::now(),
        };
        
        self.scheduler.schedule(request);
        
        // Read with error recovery
        let data = self.error_handler
            .read_with_recovery(&*self.device, sector, num_sectors)
            .await?;
        
        // Cache single sector reads
        if num_sectors == 1 {
            self.cache.put(sector, data.clone());
        }
        
        Ok(data)
    }
    
    pub fn get_cache_stats(&self) -> CacheStats {
        CacheStats {
            hit_rate: self.cache.hit_rate(),
            hits: self.cache.hit_count.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
            misses: self.cache.miss_count.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
        }
    }
}

pub struct CacheStats {
    pub hit_rate: f32,
    pub hits: u64,
    pub misses: u64,
}
```

### 12.2 Entropy-Based Sector Analysis

```rust
pub struct EntropyAnalyzer {
    window_size: usize,
}

impl EntropyAnalyzer {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        EntropyAnalyzer {
            window_size: 512,
        }
    }
    
    /// Calculate Shannon entropy of data
    /// High entropy: random/compressed data
    /// Low entropy: structured/text data
    pub fn calculate_entropy(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f32 {
        if data.is_empty() {
            return 0.0;
        }
        
        let mut frequency = [0u32; 256];
        
        for &byte in data {
            frequency[byte as usize] += 1;
        }
        
        let len = data.len() as f32;
        let mut entropy = 0.0f32;
        
        for &count in &frequency {
            if count > 0 {
                let probability = count as f32 / len;
                entropy -= probability * probability.log2();
            }
        }
        
        entropy
    }
    
    /// Analyze entropy profile to detect file types
    pub fn profile_entropy(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<f32> {
        let mut profile = Vec::new();
        
        for window_start in (0..data.len()).step_by(self.window_size) {
            let window_end = std::cmp::min(
                window_start + self.window_size,
                data.len()
            );
            let window = &data[window_start..window_end];
            profile.push(self.calculate_entropy(window));
        }
        
        profile
    }
    
    /// Detect likely file boundaries by entropy changes
    pub fn detect_boundaries(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<usize> {
        let profile = self.profile_entropy(data);
        let mut boundaries = Vec::new();
        
        for i in 1..profile.len() {
            let change = (profile[i] - profile[i - 1]).abs();
            
            // Large entropy changes indicate boundaries
            if change > 2.0 {
                boundaries.push(i * self.window_size);
            }
        }
        
        boundaries
    }
    
    /// Classify data by entropy pattern
    pub fn classify_by_entropy(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> DataClassification {
        let entropy = self.calculate_entropy(data);
        
        match entropy {
            0.0..=2.0 => DataClassification::Text,
            2.0..=4.0 => DataClassification::Structured,
            4.0..=6.0 => DataClassification::Mixed,
            6.0..=7.5 => DataClassification::Compressed,
            _ => DataClassification::Random,
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum DataClassification {
    Text,
    Structured,
    Mixed,
    Compressed,
    Random,
}
```

## 13. FILE SIGNATURE DETECTION ALGORITHMS

### 13.1 Advanced Pattern Matching

```rust
use aho_corasick::AhoCorasick;

pub struct AdvancedSignatureDetector {
    patterns: Arc<AhoCorasick>,
    signature_map: Arc<DashMap<usize, FileSignature>>,
    transition_cache: Arc<parking_lot::RwLock<TransitionCache>>,
}

pub struct TransitionCache {
    /// Maps (current_sig, next_sig) to compatibility score
    cache: std::collections::HashMap<(String, String), f32>,
}

impl AdvancedSignatureDetector {
    pub fn new(signatures: Vec<FileSignature>) -> Self {
        let patterns: Vec<Vec<u8>> = signatures
            .iter()
            .map(|s| s.magic_bytes.clone())
            .collect();
        
        let ac = AhoCorasick::new(patterns)
            .expect("Failed to build Aho-Corasick automaton");
        
        let mut signature_map = DashMap::new();
        for (idx, sig) in signatures.iter().enumerate() {
            signature_map.insert(idx, sig.clone());
        }
        
        AdvancedSignatureDetector {
            patterns: Arc::new(ac),
            signature_map: Arc::new(signature_map),
            transition_cache: Arc::new(parking_lot::RwLock::new(
                TransitionCache {
                    cache: std::collections::HashMap::new(),
                }
            )),
        }
    }
    
    /// Find all signature matches in buffer
    pub fn find_all_matches(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<SignatureMatch> {
        let mut matches = Vec::new();
        
        for mat in self.patterns.find_iter(data) {
            if let Some(sig) = self.signature_map.get(&mat.pattern()) {
                matches.push(SignatureMatch {
                    offset: mat.start(),
                    signature: sig.clone(),
                    confidence: self.calculate_confidence(
                        data,
                        mat.start(),
                        &sig
                    ),
                });
            }
        }
        
        // Score and rank matches
        matches.sort_by(|a, b| {
            b.confidence.partial_cmp(&a.confidence)
                .unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal)
        });
        
        matches
    }
    
    /// Calculate confidence score for a match
    fn calculate_confidence(
        &self,
        data: &[u8],
        offset: usize,
        sig: &FileSignature,
    ) -> f32 {
        let mut confidence = sig.confidence_base;
        
        // Bonus if footer found
        if let Some(footer) = &sig.footer_bytes {
            let search_area = std::cmp::min(
                offset + sig.typical_size as usize + 1000,
                data.len()
            );
            
            if data[offset..search_area]
                .windows(footer.len())
                .any(|w| w == footer.as_slice()) {
                confidence += 0.05;
            }
        }
        
        // Bonus based on context
        if self.has_valid_context(data, offset, sig) {
            confidence += 0.03;
        }
        
        confidence.min(1.0)
    }
    
    /// Check if surrounding context is valid
    fn has_valid_context(
        &self,
        data: &[u8],
        offset: usize,
        sig: &FileSignature,
    ) -> bool {
        if offset > 0 {
            let before = data[offset - 1];
            // Check if previous byte is null or valid separator
            if before != 0x00 && before != 0xFF {
                return false;
            }
        }
        
        let after_offset = offset + sig.magic_bytes.len();
        if after_offset < data.len() {
            let after = data[after_offset];
            // Next byte should be valid for file type
            !matches!(after, 0x00 | 0xFF | 0xFE)
        } else {
            true
        }
    }
    
    /// Filter overlapping matches, keeping best ones
    pub fn resolve_overlaps(
        &self,
        mut matches: Vec<SignatureMatch>,
    ) -> Vec<SignatureMatch> {
        matches.sort_by_key(|m| m.offset);
        
        let mut resolved = Vec::new();
        let mut last_end = 0;
        
        for mat in matches {
            let estimated_end = mat.offset + mat.signature.typical_size as usize;
            
            if mat.offset >= last_end {
                last_end = estimated_end;
                resolved.push(mat);
            }
        }
        
        resolved
    }
}

pub struct SignatureMatch {
    pub offset: usize,
    pub signature: FileSignature,
    pub confidence: f32,
}
```

### 13.2 Regex-Based Signature Detection

```rust
use regex::bytes::Regex;

pub struct RegexSignatureDetector {
    patterns: Arc<Vec<(Regex, FileSignature)>>,
}

impl RegexSignatureDetector {
    pub fn new(signatures: Vec<FileSignature>) -> Result<Self> {
        let mut patterns = Vec::new();
        
        for sig in signatures {
            // Convert pattern to regex if not already
            let regex_pattern = if sig.pattern.contains("[") {
                sig.pattern.clone()
            } else {
                // Convert simple hex pattern to regex
                format!("(?-u:{})", sig.pattern)
            };
            
            let re = Regex::new(&regex_pattern)?;
            patterns.push((re, sig));
        }
        
        Ok(RegexSignatureDetector {
            patterns: Arc::new(patterns),
        })
    }
    
    pub fn find_matches(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<RegexMatch> {
        let mut matches = Vec::new();
        
        for (regex, sig) in self.patterns.iter() {
            for mat in regex.find_iter(data) {
                matches.push(RegexMatch {
                    offset: mat.start(),
                    length: mat.len(),
                    signature: sig.clone(),
                });
            }
        }
        
        matches
    }
}

pub struct RegexMatch {
    pub offset: usize,
    pub length: usize,
    pub signature: FileSignature,
}
```

## 14. FRAGMENTATION HANDLING ALGORITHMS

### 14.1 Fragmentation Detection & Analysis

```rust
pub struct FragmentationAnalyzer {
    max_gap_threshold: u64,
    similarity_threshold: f32,
}

pub struct Fragment {
    pub start_sector: u64,
    pub end_sector: u64,
    pub size: u64,
    pub content_hash: String,
    pub entropy: f32,
}

pub struct FragmentationPattern {
    pub fragments: Vec<Fragment>,
    pub total_sectors: u64,
    pub gap_sizes: Vec<u64>,
    pub fragmentation_ratio: f32,
    pub predicted_file_type: Option<String>,
}

impl FragmentationAnalyzer {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        FragmentationAnalyzer {
            max_gap_threshold: 100, // Max gap before considering separate file
            similarity_threshold: 0.85,
        }
    }
    
    /// Analyze fragmentation pattern
    pub fn analyze_fragments(
        &self,
        candidates: &[FileCand idate],
    ) -> Vec<FragmentationPattern> {
        let mut patterns = Vec::new();
        let mut processed = std::collections::HashSet::new();
        
        for start_candidate in candidates {
            if processed.contains(&start_candidate.sector_offset) {
                continue;
            }
            
            let pattern = self.build_pattern(
                start_candidate,
                candidates,
                &mut processed,
            );
            
            patterns.push(pattern);
        }
        
        patterns
    }
    
    fn build_pattern(
        &self,
        start: &FileCandidate,
        all_candidates: &[FileCandidate],
        processed: &mut std::collections::HashSet<u64>,
    ) -> FragmentationPattern {
        let mut fragments = Vec::new();
        let mut gap_sizes = Vec::new();
        
        let mut current_sector = start.sector_offset;
        let mut last_end = start.sector_offset;
        
        for candidate in all_candidates {
            // Check if this candidate is part of same file
            let gap = candidate.sector_offset.saturating_sub(last_end);
            
            if gap <= self.max_gap_threshold 
                && candidate.signature.file_type 
                == start.signature.file_type {
                
                // Add gap if non-zero
                if gap > 0 {
                    gap_sizes.push(gap);
                }
                
                fragments.push(Fragment {
                    start_sector: candidate.sector_offset,
                    end_sector: candidate.sector_offset + 1,
                    size: 1,
                    content_hash: String::new(),
                    entropy: candidate.confidence,
                });
                
                last_end = candidate.sector_offset + 1;
                processed.insert(candidate.sector_offset);
            }
        }
        
        let total_sectors: u64 = fragments
            .iter()
            .map(|f| f.size)
            .sum();
        
        let total_gap: u64 = gap_sizes.iter().sum();
        let fragmentation_ratio = if total_sectors + total_gap > 0 {
            total_gap as f32 / (total_sectors + total_gap) as f32
        } else {
            0.0
        };
        
        FragmentationPattern {
            fragments,
            total_sectors,
            gap_sizes,
            fragmentation_ratio,
            predicted_file_type: Some(
                start.signature.file_type.clone()
            ),
        }
    }
    
    /// Predict how fragments should be ordered
    pub fn predict_fragment_order(
        &self,
        fragments: &[Fragment],
    ) -> Vec<usize> {
        // Use heuristics to order fragments
        
        let mut indices: Vec<usize> = (0..fragments.len()).collect();
        
        // Sort by entropy pattern (more structured files first)
        indices.sort_by(|&a, &b| {
            fragments[a].entropy.partial_cmp(&fragments[b].entropy)
                .unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal)
        });
        
        indices
    }
    
    /// Detect if fragments belong to same file
    pub fn fragments_belong_together(
        &self,
        frag1: &Fragment,
        frag2: &Fragment,
    ) -> f32 {
        // Score how likely fragments belong together
        
        let mut score = 1.0f32;
        
        // Penalty for large gaps
        let gap = frag2.start_sector.saturating_sub(frag1.end_sector);
        if gap > self.max_gap_threshold {
            score *= 0.5;
        } else if gap > 10 {
            score *= 0.9;
        }
        
        // Bonus for similar entropy
        let entropy_diff = (frag1.entropy - frag2.entropy).abs();
        if entropy_diff < 0.1 {
            score *= 1.1;
        }
        
        score.min(1.0)
    }
}
```

### 14.2 Fragment Reassembly Algorithm

```rust
pub struct FragmentReassembler {
    analyzer: Arc<FragmentationAnalyzer>,
}

pub struct ReassemblyResult {
    pub complete: bool,
    pub missing_percentage: f32,
    pub reassembled_data: Vec<u8>,
    pub fragment_order: Vec<usize>,
    pub confidence: f32,
}

impl FragmentReassembler {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        FragmentReassembler {
            analyzer: Arc::new(FragmentationAnalyzer::new()),
        }
    }
    
    /// Attempt to reassemble fragmented file
    pub async fn reassemble(
        &self,
        fragments: Vec<Fragment>,
        device: &dyn StorageDevice,
    ) -> Result<ReassemblyResult> {
        if fragments.is_empty() {
            return Err("No fragments to reassemble".into());
        }
        
        // Step 1: Determine likely order
        let order = self.determine_order(&fragments);
        
        // Step 2: Read and concatenate fragments
        let mut reassembled = Vec::new();
        let mut total_expected_size = 0u64;
        
        for &idx in &order {
            let frag = &fragments[idx];
            let data = device.read_sectors(
                frag.start_sector,
                frag.size,
            )?;
            reassembled.extend_from_slice(&data);
            total_expected_size += frag.size * device.get_sector_size() as u64;
        }
        
        // Step 3: Fill gaps if possible
        self.attempt_gap_filling(&mut reassembled, &fragments);
        
        // Step 4: Calculate success metrics
        let missing_percentage = if total_expected_size > 0 {
            ((total_expected_size - reassembled.len() as u64) 
                as f32 / total_expected_size as f32) * 100.0
        } else {
            0.0
        };
        
        let confidence = 1.0 - (missing_percentage / 100.0);
        
        Ok(ReassemblyResult {
            complete: missing_percentage < 5.0,
            missing_percentage,
            reassembled_data: reassembled,
            fragment_order: order,
            confidence,
        })
    }
    
    /// Determine optimal fragment order using heuristics
    fn determine_order(&self, fragments: &[Fragment]) -> Vec<usize> {
        let mut indices: Vec<usize> = (0..fragments.len()).collect();
        
        // Build adjacency graph
        let mut scores: Vec<Vec<f32>> = vec![
            vec![0.0; fragments.len()]; 
            fragments.len()
        ];
        
        for i in 0..fragments.len() {
            for j in 0..fragments.len() {
                if i != j {
                    scores[i][j] = self.analyzer
                        .fragments_belong_together(
                            &fragments[i],
                            &fragments[j],
                        );
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Greedy nearest-neighbor ordering
        let mut ordered = vec![0];
        let mut remaining: std::collections::HashSet<_> = 
            (1..fragments.len()).collect();
        
        while !remaining.is_empty() {
            let last = *ordered.last().unwrap();
            let next = remaining
                .iter()
                .max_by(|&&a, &&b| {
                    scores[last][a]
                        .partial_cmp(&scores[last][b])
                        .unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal)
                })
                .copied()
                .unwrap();
            
            ordered.push(next);
            remaining.remove(&next);
        }
        
        ordered
    }
    
    /// Attempt to fill gaps in reassembled data
    fn attempt_gap_filling(
        &self,
        data: &mut Vec<u8>,
        fragments: &[Fragment],
    ) {
        // Look for patterns that might fill gaps
        
        // Pattern 1: Null byte padding
        if data.iter().all(|&b| b == 0) {
            // Likely all null padding, can fill
            return;
        }
        
        // Pattern 2: Repeated pattern
        let possible_pattern = Self::detect_pattern(data, 16);
        if let Some(pattern) = possible_pattern {
            self.fill_with_pattern(data, &pattern);
        }
    }
    
    fn detect_pattern(data: &[u8], max_len: usize) -> Option<Vec<u8>> {
        for pattern_len in 1..=std::cmp::min(max_len, data.len() / 2) {
            let pattern = &data[0..pattern_len];
            
            let matches = data
                .chunks(pattern_len)
                .take(10)
                .all(|chunk| {
                    chunk.len() < pattern_len 
                    || chunk == pattern
                });
            
            if matches {
                return Some(pattern.to_vec());
            }
        }
        
        None
    }
    
    fn fill_with_pattern(&self, data: &mut Vec<u8>, pattern: &[u8]) {
        let target_len = data.len() + 1024; // Extend by 1KB
        
        while data.len() < target_len {
            for &byte in pattern {
                data.push(byte);
                if data.len() >= target_len {
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

## 15. HEURISTIC ANALYSIS & MACHINE LEARNING

### 15.1 ML-Based File Type Classification

```rust
use tch::{nn, nn::OptimizerConfig, Device, Tensor};

pub struct MLFileClassifier {
    model: nn::Sequential,
    feature_extractor: Arc<FeatureExtractor>,
    class_labels: Arc<Vec<String>>,
}

pub struct FeatureExtractor {
    feature_size: usize,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct FileFeatures {
    pub byte_distribution: [f32; 256],
    pub entropy: f32,
    pub compression_ratio: f32,
    pub magic_bytes_score: f32,
    pub structural_score: f32,
}

impl FeatureExtractor {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        FeatureExtractor {
            feature_size: 256 + 4, // byte dist + 4 other features
        }
    }
    
    /// Extract features from file data
    pub fn extract(&self, data: &[u8]) -> FileFeatures {
        // Byte distribution (first 256 features)
        let mut byte_dist = [0.0f32; 256];
        let sample_size = std::cmp::min(4096, data.len());
        
        for &byte in &data[..sample_size] {
            byte_dist[byte as usize] += 1.0;
        }
        
        let sum: f32 = byte_dist.iter().sum();
        if sum > 0.0 {
            for f in &mut byte_dist {
                *f /= sum;
            }
        }
        
        // Entropy
        let entropy = self.calculate_entropy(data);
        
        // Compression ratio (how compressible)
        let compression_ratio = self.estimate_compression(data);
        
        // Magic bytes score
        let magic_bytes_score = self.magic_bytes_score(data);
        
        // Structural score (detecting structured formats)
        let structural_score = self.detect_structure(data);
        
        FileFeatures {
            byte_distribution: byte_dist,
            entropy,
            compression_ratio,
            magic_bytes_score,
            structural_score,
        }
    }
    
    fn calculate_entropy(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f32 {
        let mut freq = [0u32; 256];
        let sample_size = std::cmp::min(4096, data.len());
        
        for &byte in &data[..sample_size] {
            freq[byte as usize] += 1;
        }
        
        let len = sample_size as f32;
        let mut entropy = 0.0f32;
        
        for &count in &freq {
            if count > 0 {
                let p = count as f32 / len;
                entropy -= p * p.log2();
            }
        }
        
        entropy / 8.0 // Normalize to 0-1
    }
    
    fn estimate_compression(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f32 {
        // Simple RLE compression estimation
        let sample = &data[..std::cmp::min(1024, data.len())];
        let mut runs = 0;
        let mut last_byte = sample[0];
        
        for &byte in &sample[1..] {
            if byte != last_byte {
                runs += 1;
                last_byte = byte;
            }
        }
        
        let compression_ratio = runs as f32 / sample.len() as f32;
        compression_ratio.min(1.0)
    }
    
    fn magic_bytes_score(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f32 {
        if data.len() < 4 {
            return 0.0;
        }
        
        // Known file signatures
        match &data[0..std::cmp::min(4, data.len())] {
            b"\xFF\xD8\xFF" => 0.95,  // JPEG
            b"\x89PNG" => 0.98,        // PNG
            b"%PDF" => 0.96,           // PDF
            b"PK\x03\x04" => 0.94,     // ZIP
            _ => 0.3,
        }
    }
    
    fn detect_structure(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f32 {
        // Detect structured vs random data
        let sample = &data[..std::cmp::min(512, data.len())];
        
        let printable = sample
            .iter()
            .filter(|&&b| b >= 32 && b <= 126)
            .count() as f32 / sample.len() as f32;
        
        let nulls = sample
            .iter()
            .filter(|&&b| b == 0)
            .count() as f32 / sample.len() as f32;
        
        // High printable + some nulls = likely structure
        (printable * 0.6 + (1.0 - nulls) * 0.4).min(1.0)
    }
    
    pub fn features_to_tensor(&self, features: &FileFeatures) 
        -> Tensor {
        let mut values = Vec::with_capacity(self.feature_size);
        values.extend_from_slice(&features.byte_distribution);
        values.push(features.entropy);
        values.push(features.compression_ratio);
        values.push(features.magic_bytes_score);
        values.push(features.structural_score);
        
        Tensor::of_slice(&values)
    }
}

impl MLFileClassifier {
    pub fn new(device: Device) -> Result<Self> {
        let vs = nn::VarStore::new(device);
        let root = vs.root();
        
        let model = nn::seq(&root, |p| {
            p.func_res(|p| {
                // Input layer: 260 features
                // Hidden layers: 128 -> 64 -> 32
                // Output layer: 50 file types
                
                let layer1 = nn::linear(p, 260, 128, Default::default());
                let layer2 = nn::linear(p, 128, 64, Default::default());
                let layer3 = nn::linear(p, 64, 32, Default::default());
                let output = nn::linear(p, 32, 50, Default::default());
                
                Ok(nn::seq(p, |_| {
                    // Would implement forward pass here
                }))
            })
        })?;
        
        Ok(MLFileClassifier {
            model,
            feature_extractor: Arc::new(FeatureExtractor::new()),
            class_labels: Arc::new(vec![
                "JPEG".to_string(),
                "PNG".to_string(),
                "PDF".to_string(),
                "ZIP".to_string(),
                // ... 46 more file types
            ]),
        })
    }
    
    pub fn classify(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<(String, f32)> {
        // Extract features
        let features = self.feature_extractor.extract(data);
        
        // Convert to tensor
        let input = self.feature_extractor
            .features_to_tensor(&features);
        
        // Run through model
        // let output = self.model.forward(&input);
        
        // Get top prediction
        // let (class_idx, confidence) = output.top_class();
        
        // For now, return placeholder
        Ok(("Unknown".to_string(), 0.5))
    }
    
    pub fn batch_classify(
        &self,
        items: Vec<Vec<u8>>,
    ) -> Result<Vec<(String, f32)>> {
        let mut results = Vec::new();
        
        for data in items {
            results.push(self.classify(&data)?);
        }
        
        Ok(results)
    }
}

/// Training module for ML classifier
pub mod training {
    use super::*;
    
    pub struct TrainingData {

    }
    
    pub struct Trainer {
```

### 15.2 Heuristic Scoring System

```rust
pub struct HeuristicScorer {
    rules: Arc<Vec<ScoringRule>>,
}

pub struct ScoringRule {
    pub name: String,
    pub weight: f32,
    pub evaluator: Box<dyn Fn(&[u8]) -> f32 + Send + Sync>,
}

impl HeuristicScorer {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        HeuristicScorer {
            rules: Arc::new(vec![
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "magic_bytes_present".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.15,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        if data.len() < 4 { return 0.0; }
                        match &data[0..4] {
                            b"\xFF\xD8\xFF" | b"\x89PNG" 
                            | b"%PDF" | b"PK\x03" => 1.0,
                            _ => 0.0,
                        }
                    }),
                },
                
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "entropy_consistent".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.10,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        let mut freq = [0u32; 256];
                        for &byte in data.iter().take(512) {
                            freq[byte as usize] += 1;
                        }
                        
                        let len = std::cmp::min(512, data.len()) as f32;
                        let mut entropy = 0.0f32;
                        
                        for &count in &freq {
                            if count > 0 {
                                let p = count as f32 / len;
                                entropy -= p * p.log2();
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // Entropy between 4-7 is good
                        if entropy >= 4.0 && entropy <= 7.0 {
                            1.0
                        } else {
                            0.5
                        }
                    }),
                },
                
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "valid_structure".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.20,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        if data.len() < 512 { return 0.5; }
                        
                        let printable = data[..512]
                            .iter()
                            .filter(|&&b| b >= 32 && b <= 126 || b == b'\n')
                            .count() as f32 / 512.0;
                        
                        if printable > 0.7 { 1.0 }
                        else if printable > 0.3 { 0.7 }
                        else { 0.3 }
                    }),
                },
                
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "size_reasonable".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.10,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        match data.len() {
                            0..=512 => 0.7,      // Very small
                            513..=1_000_000 => 1.0,
                            1_000_001..=1_000_000_000 => 0.9,
                            _ => 0.6,            // Very large
                        }
                    }),
                },
                
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "no_obvious_corruption".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.15,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        if data.is_empty() { return 0.0; }
                        
                        let all_same = data.iter()
                            .all(|&b| b == data[0]);
                        
                        if all_same { 0.2 }
                        else { 1.0 }
                    }),
                },
                
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "contains_metadata".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.15,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        // Look for common metadata patterns
                        let has_utf8_text = String::from_utf8_lossy(data)
                            .len() > data.len() / 4;
                        
                        if has_utf8_text { 1.0 } else { 0.5 }
                    }),
                },
                
                ScoringRule {
                    name: "recoverable_type".to_string(),
                    weight: 0.15,
                    evaluator: Box::new(|data| {
                        if data.len() < 4 { return 0.3; }
                        
                        // Common recoverable types get higher score
                        match &data[0..std::cmp::min(4, data.len())] {
                            b"\xFF\xD8\xFF" => 0.95,  // JPEG - very recoverable
                            b"\x89PNG" => 0.95,        // PNG
                            b"%PDF" => 0.92,           // PDF
                            b"PK\x03\x04" => 0.90,     // ZIP
                            _ => 0.60,
                        }
                    }),
                },
            ]),
        }
    }
    
    /// Calculate composite score for file recovery likelihood
    pub fn score_recovery_likelihood(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> f32 {
        let mut total_score = 0.0f32;
        let mut total_weight = 0.0f32;
        
        for rule in self.rules.iter() {
            let rule_score = (rule.evaluator)(data);
            total_score += rule_score * rule.weight;
            total_weight += rule.weight;
        }
        
        if total_weight > 0.0 {
            total_score / total_weight
        } else {
            0.0
        }
    }
    
    /// Get detailed scoring breakdown
    pub fn score_with_details(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Vec<(String, f32)> {
        self.rules
            .iter()
            .map(|rule| {
                let score = (rule.evaluator)(data);
                (rule.name.clone(), score)
            })
            .collect()
    }
}
```

# SECTION IV: DATABASE & DATA STRUCTURES

## 16. DATABASE SCHEMA DESIGN

### 16.1 Core SQLite Schema

```sql
-- ============================================================================
-- SCANS TABLE - Records all scan operations
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS scans (
    scan_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    device_path TEXT NOT NULL,
    device_name TEXT,
    file_system_type TEXT,
    scan_start_time INTEGER NOT NULL, -- Unix timestamp
    scan_end_time INTEGER,
    scan_duration_ms INTEGER,
    scan_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'quick', 'normal', 'deep'
    files_found INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_size_scanned INTEGER,
    is_completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_cancelled BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    error_message TEXT,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL
);

CREATE INDEX idx_scans_device_time 
    ON scans(device_path, scan_start_time DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_scans_completed 
    ON scans(is_completed, created_at DESC);

-- ============================================================================
-- SCAN_RESULTS TABLE - Individual files found during scans
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS scan_results (
    result_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    scan_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    file_type TEXT NOT NULL,
    file_signature TEXT,
    estimated_size INTEGER,
    first_sector INTEGER,
    last_verified_sector INTEGER,
    recovery_confidence REAL,
    recovery_confidence_reason TEXT,
    fragmentation_level REAL,
    is_fragmented BOOLEAN,
    file_name TEXT,
    original_name TEXT,
    entropy REAL,
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending', -- 'pending', 'recovering', 'recovered', 'failed', 'skipped'
    recovery_notes TEXT,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    
    FOREIGN KEY(scan_id) REFERENCES scans(scan_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_scan_results_scan 
    ON scan_results(scan_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_scan_results_type 
    ON scan_results(file_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_scan_results_status 
    ON scan_results(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_scan_results_confidence 
    ON scan_results(recovery_confidence DESC);

-- ============================================================================
-- RECOVERED_FILES TABLE - Files that have been recovered
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS recovered_files (
    recovery_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    result_id TEXT,
    scan_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    destination_path TEXT NOT NULL,
    original_file_size INTEGER,
    recovered_file_size INTEGER,
    recovery_timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL,
    recovery_duration_ms INTEGER,
    recovery_strategy TEXT, -- 'metadata_based', 'signature_based', 'carving'
    file_hash TEXT, -- SHA-256
    file_hash_md5 TEXT, -- For quick comparison
    integrity_status TEXT, -- 'perfect', 'good', 'fair', 'poor', 'corrupted'
    integrity_score REAL, -- 0.0-1.0
    integrity_details TEXT, -- JSON with detailed validation results
    is_openable BOOLEAN,
    recovery_notes TEXT,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    
    FOREIGN KEY(result_id) REFERENCES scan_results(result_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(scan_id) REFERENCES scans(scan_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_recovered_timestamp 
    ON recovered_files(recovery_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_recovered_scan 
    ON recovered_files(scan_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_recovered_hash 
    ON recovered_files(file_hash);

-- ============================================================================
-- FILE_SIGNATURES TABLE - Database of known file signatures
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS file_signatures (
    signature_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    file_type TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    magic_bytes BLOB,
    magic_bytes_hex TEXT,
    footer_bytes BLOB,
    footer_bytes_hex TEXT,
    header_pattern TEXT,
    min_file_size INTEGER,
    max_file_size INTEGER,
    typical_size INTEGER,
    confidence_score REAL,
    description TEXT,
    extensions TEXT, -- comma-separated list
    mime_types TEXT,
    is_recoverable BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    recovery_notes TEXT,
    updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL
);

CREATE INDEX idx_signatures_type ON file_signatures(file_type);

-- Sample data
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO file_signatures (
    signature_id, file_type, magic_bytes_hex, footer_bytes_hex,
    min_file_size, typical_size, max_file_size, confidence_score,
    extensions, mime_types, updated_at
) VALUES
    ('jpeg-sig', 'JPEG', 'FFD8FFES', 'FFD9', 1000, 2000000, 500000000, 0.95,
     'jpg,jpeg,jpe', 'image/jpeg', 0),
    ('png-sig', 'PNG', '89504E47', '49454E44', 1000, 1000000, 1000000000, 0.98,
     'png', 'image/png', 0),
    ('pdf-sig', 'PDF', '25504446', '25254541460A', 1000, 1000000, 2000000000, 0.96,
     'pdf', 'application/pdf', 0),
    ('zip-sig', 'ZIP', '504B0304', '504B0506', 1000, 5000000, 5000000000, 0.92,
     'zip', 'application/zip', 0);

-- ============================================================================
-- DEVICE_CACHE TABLE - Caching for device performance
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS device_cache (
    cache_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    device_path TEXT NOT NULL,
    cache_key TEXT NOT NULL,
    cache_value BLOB,
    value_type TEXT, -- 'sector_data', 'metadata', 'fs_info'
    expiration_time INTEGER,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    
    UNIQUE(device_path, cache_key)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_cache_expiration 
    ON device_cache(expiration_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_cache_device 
    ON device_cache(device_path);

-- ============================================================================
-- SCAN_STATISTICS TABLE - Analytics and metrics
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS scan_statistics (
    stat_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    scan_id TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    files_by_type TEXT, -- JSON: {"JPEG": 100, "PNG": 50, ...}
    recovery_confidence_dist TEXT, -- JSON: {"0.9-1.0": 500, ...}
    fragmentation_stats TEXT, -- JSON with fragmentation details
    avg_file_size REAL,
    total_recoverable_size INTEGER,
    estimated_recovery_time_ms INTEGER,
    scan_speed_mbps REAL,
    device_health_status TEXT, -- 'healthy', 'degraded', 'failing'
    
    FOREIGN KEY(scan_id) REFERENCES scans(scan_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- ============================================================================
-- DEDUPLICATION_HASHES TABLE - For finding duplicate files
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS deduplication_hashes (
    hash_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    sha256_hash TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    md5_hash TEXT,
    file_size INTEGER,
    file_type TEXT,
    first_occurrence INTEGER, -- scan_id
    duplicate_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL
);

CREATE INDEX idx_dedup_sha256 ON deduplication_hashes(sha256_hash);
CREATE INDEX idx_dedup_size ON deduplication_hashes(file_size);

-- ============================================================================
-- RECOVERY_QUEUE TABLE - Scheduled recovery operations
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS recovery_queue (
    queue_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    result_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    priority INTEGER DEFAULT 50, -- 0-100
    scheduled_time INTEGER,
    retry_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    max_retries INTEGER DEFAULT 3,
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending', -- 'pending', 'processing', 'completed', 'failed'
    error_message TEXT,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    started_at INTEGER,
    completed_at INTEGER,
    
    FOREIGN KEY(result_id) REFERENCES scan_results(result_id)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_queue_priority 
    ON recovery_queue(priority DESC, created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_queue_status 
    ON recovery_queue(status);

-- ============================================================================
-- AUDIT_LOG TABLE - Compliance and security logging
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_log (
    log_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    operation TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'scan', 'recover', 'delete', 'export'
    entity_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'scan', 'file', 'device'
    entity_id TEXT,
    user_id TEXT,
    status TEXT, -- 'success', 'failure'
    details TEXT, -- JSON with operation details
    timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL,
    ip_address TEXT
);

CREATE INDEX idx_audit_timestamp 
    ON audit_log(timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_operation 
    ON audit_log(operation);
Create INDEX idx_audit_entity 
    ON audit_log(entity_type, entity_id);

-- ============================================================================
-- PREFERENCES TABLE - User settings
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS preferences (
    pref_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    theme TEXT DEFAULT 'light',
    auto_scan_on_connect BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    default_recovery_destination TEXT,
    skip_system_files BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    min_file_size INTEGER DEFAULT 1024,
    max_file_size INTEGER DEFAULT -1, -- -1 = unlimited
    default_scan_type TEXT DEFAULT 'normal',
    language TEXT DEFAULT 'en',
    notification_level TEXT DEFAULT 'normal',
    enable_cloud_backup BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
    updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL
);

-- ============================================================================
-- SETTINGS TABLE - Application configuration
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS settings (
    setting_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    setting_name TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    setting_value TEXT,
    setting_type TEXT, -- 'string', 'integer', 'boolean', 'json'
    is_sensitive BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL
);

-- ============================================================================
-- FILE_FRAGMENTS TABLE - Detailed fragmentation tracking
-- ============================================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS file_fragments (
    fragment_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    result_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    fragment_index INTEGER,
    start_sector INTEGER NOT NULL,
    end_sector INTEGER NOT NULL,
    size_bytes INTEGER,
    confidence REAL,
    
    FOREIGN KEY(result_id) REFERENCES scan_results(result_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_fragments_result 
    ON file_fragments(result_id);

-- ============================================================================
-- VIEWS for easier querying
-- ============================================================================

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_recovery_summary AS
SELECT 
    s.scan_id,
    s.device_path,
    COUNT(sr.result_id) as total_files,
    SUM(CASE WHEN sr.status = 'recovered' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as recovered_files,
    SUM(sr.estimated_size) as total_size,
    SUM(CASE WHEN rf.recovery_id IS NOT NULL THEN rf.recovered_file_size ELSE 0 END) as total_recovered,
    AVG(sr.recovery_confidence) as avg_confidence
FROM scans s
LEFT JOIN scan_results sr ON s.scan_id = sr.scan_id
LEFT JOIN recovered_files rf ON sr.result_id = rf.result_id
GROUP BY s.scan_id;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_file_type_stats AS
SELECT 
    file_type,
    COUNT(*) as count,
    SUM(estimated_size) as total_size,
    AVG(recovery_confidence) as avg_confidence,
    SUM(CASE WHEN is_fragmented = TRUE THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as fragmented_count
FROM scan_results
WHERE status != 'skipped'
GROUP BY file_type
ORDER BY count DESC;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_failed_recoveries AS
SELECT 
    rf.recovery_id,
    sr.file_type,
    rf.destination_path,
    rf.integrity_score,
    rf.recovery_strategy,
    rf.recovery_notes
FROM recovered_files rf
JOIN scan_results sr ON rf.result_id = sr.result_id
WHERE rf.integrity_status IN ('poor', 'corrupted')
ORDER BY rf.recovery_timestamp DESC;
```

### 16.2 Rust Database Abstraction Layer

```rust
use sqlx::{SqlitePool, Row, sqlite::SqliteConnectOptions};
use std::str::FromStr;

pub struct Database {
    pool: SqlitePool,
    schema_version: i32,
}

impl Database {
    /// Initialize database connection pool
    pub async fn new(database_url: &str) -> Result<Self> {
        // Create connection options
        let connect_options = SqliteConnectOptions::from_str(database_url)?
            .create_if_missing(true);
        
        // Create connection pool
        let pool = SqlitePool::connect_with(
            sqlx::sqlite::SqlitePoolOptions::new()
                .max_connections(10)
                .connect_with(connect_options)
        ).await?;
        
        // Initialize schema
        let db = Database {
            pool,
            schema_version: 1,
        };
        
        db.init_schema().await?;
        
        Ok(db)
    }
    
    /// Initialize database schema
    async fn init_schema(&self) -> Result<()> {
        // Run schema migration SQL
        sqlx::query(include_str!("schema.sql"))
            .execute(&self.pool)
            .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Create a new scan record
    pub async fn create_scan(
        &self,
        scan_id: &str,
        device_path: &str,
        device_name: &str,
        scan_type: &str,
    ) -> Result<()> {
        let now = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)?
            .as_secs() as i64;
        
        sqlx::query(
            "INSERT INTO scans (scan_id, device_path, device_name, scan_start_time, scan_type, created_at, updated_at)
             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)"
        )
        .bind(scan_id)
        .bind(device_path)
        .bind(device_name)
        .bind(now)
        .bind(scan_type)
        .bind(now)
        .bind(now)
        .execute(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Add scan result (found file)
    pub async fn add_scan_result(
        &self,
        result: &ScanResultRecord,
    ) -> Result<()> {
        sqlx::query(
            "INSERT INTO scan_results 
            (result_id, scan_id, file_type, file_signature, estimated_size, 
             first_sector, recovery_confidence, fragmentation_level, 
             entropy, status, created_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)"
        )
        .bind(&result.result_id)
        .bind(&result.scan_id)
        .bind(&result.file_type)
        .bind(&result.file_signature)
        .bind(result.estimated_size)
        .bind(result.first_sector)
        .bind(result.recovery_confidence)
        .bind(result.fragmentation_level)
        .bind(result.entropy)
        .bind("pending")
        .bind(
            std::time::SystemTime::now()
                .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)?
                .as_secs() as i64
        )
        .execute(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Record recovered file
    pub async fn record_recovery(
        &self,
        recovery: &RecoveryRecord,
    ) -> Result<()> {
        let now = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)?
            .as_secs() as i64;
        
        sqlx::query(
            "INSERT INTO recovered_files 
            (recovery_id, result_id, scan_id, destination_path, 
             original_file_size, recovered_file_size, recovery_timestamp,
             recovery_strategy, file_hash, integrity_status, 
             integrity_score, created_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)"
        )
        .bind(&recovery.recovery_id)
        .bind(&recovery.result_id)
        .bind(&recovery.scan_id)
        .bind(&recovery.destination_path)
        .bind(recovery.original_size)
        .bind(recovery.recovered_size)
        .bind(now)
        .bind(&recovery.strategy)
        .bind(&recovery.file_hash)
        .bind(&recovery.integrity_status)
        .bind(recovery.integrity_score)
        .bind(now)
        .execute(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        // Update scan_results status
        sqlx::query(
            "UPDATE scan_results SET status = 'recovered' WHERE result_id = ?"
        )
        .bind(&recovery.result_id)
        .execute(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Get all scans for a device
    pub async fn get_device_scans(&self, device_path: &str) 
        -> Result<Vec<ScanRecord>> {
        let records = sqlx::query(
            "SELECT scan_id, device_path, device_name, scan_start_time, 
                    scan_end_time, files_found, is_completed
             FROM scans WHERE device_path = ? ORDER BY scan_start_time DESC"
        )
        .bind(device_path)
        .fetch_all(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        let scans = records
            .iter()
            .map(|row| ScanRecord {
                scan_id: row.get(0),
                device_path: row.get(1),
                device_name: row.get(2),
                scan_start_time: row.get(3),
                scan_end_time: row.get(4),
                files_found: row.get(5),
                is_completed: row.get(6),
            })
            .collect();
        
        Ok(scans)
    }
    
    /// Get scan results with filtering
    pub async fn get_scan_results(
        &self,
        scan_id: &str,
        filters: &ResultFilters,
    ) -> Result<Vec<ScanResultRecord>> {
        let mut query = 
            "SELECT result_id, scan_id, file_type, estimated_size, first_sector, 
                    recovery_confidence, fragmentation_level, entropy, status
             FROM scan_results WHERE scan_id = ?".to_string();
        
        let mut query_builder = sqlx::query_as::<_, ScanResultRecord>(
            &query
        ).bind(scan_id);
        
        // Apply filters
        if let Some(file_types) = &filters.file_types {
            if !file_types.is_empty() {
                let placeholders = file_types
                    .iter()
                    .map(|_| "?")
                    .collect::<Vec<_>>()
                    .join(",");
                
                query.push_str(&format!(" AND file_type IN ({})", placeholders));
                
                for ft in file_types {
                    query_builder = query_builder.bind(ft);
                }
            }
        }
        
        if let Some(min_confidence) = filters.min_confidence {
            query.push_str(" AND recovery_confidence >= ?");
            query_builder = query_builder.bind(min_confidence);
        }
        
        if let Some(status) = &filters.status {
            query.push_str(" AND status = ?");
            query_builder = query_builder.bind(status);
        }
        
        query.push_str(" ORDER BY recovery_confidence DESC");
        
        let records = sqlx::query_as::<_, ScanResultRecord>(&query)
            .bind(scan_id)
            .fetch_all(&self.pool)
            .await?;
        
        Ok(records)
    }
    
    /// Get recovery statistics for a scan
    pub async fn get_recovery_stats(&self, scan_id: &str) 
        -> Result<RecoveryStats> {
        let row = sqlx::query(
            "SELECT 
                COUNT(*) as total_files,
                SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'recovered' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as recovered,
                SUM(estimated_size) as total_size,
                AVG(recovery_confidence) as avg_confidence
             FROM scan_results WHERE scan_id = ?"
        )
        .bind(scan_id)
        .fetch_one(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(RecoveryStats {
            total_files: row.get(0),
            recovered_files: row.get(1),
            total_size: row.get(2),
            avg_confidence: row.get(3),
        })
    }
    
    /// Cache sector data
    pub async fn cache_sector_data(
        &self,
        device_path: &str,
        sector: u64,
        data: &[u8],
    ) -> Result<()> {
        let cache_id = format!("{}-{}", device_path, sector);
        let now = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)?
            .as_secs() as i64;
        let expiration = now + 3600; // 1 hour cache
        
        sqlx::query(
            "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO device_cache 
            (cache_id, device_path, cache_key, cache_value, value_type, 
             expiration_time, created_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)"
        )
        .bind(&cache_id)
        .bind(device_path)
        .bind(sector.to_string())
        .bind(data)
        .bind("sector_data")
        .bind(expiration)
        .bind(now)
        .execute(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Get cached sector data
    pub async fn get_cached_sector(
        &self,
        device_path: &str,
        sector: u64,
    ) -> Result<Option<Vec<u8>>> {
        let now = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)?
            .as_secs() as i64;
        
        let row = sqlx::query(
            "SELECT cache_value FROM device_cache 
             WHERE device_path = ? AND cache_key = ? AND expiration_time > ?"
        )
        .bind(device_path)
        .bind(sector.to_string())
        .bind(now)
        .fetch_optional(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(row.map(|r| r.get(0)))
    }
    
    /// Add audit log entry
    pub async fn log_audit(
        &self,
        operation: &str,
        entity_type: &str,
        entity_id: &str,
        status: &str,
        details: &str,
    ) -> Result<()> {
        let now = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)?
            .as_secs() as i64;
        
        let log_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();
        
        sqlx::query(
            "INSERT INTO audit_log 
            (log_id, operation, entity_type, entity_id, status, details, timestamp)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)"
        )
        .bind(&log_id)
        .bind(operation)
        .bind(entity_type)
        .bind(entity_id)
        .bind(status)
        .bind(details)
        .bind(now)
        .execute(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Get file type statistics
    pub async fn get_file_type_stats(&self, scan_id: &str) 
        -> Result<Vec<FileTypeStats>> {
        let rows = sqlx::query(
            "SELECT file_type, COUNT(*) as count, 
                    SUM(estimated_size) as total_size,
                    AVG(recovery_confidence) as avg_confidence
             FROM scan_results WHERE scan_id = ?
             GROUP BY file_type ORDER BY count DESC"
        )
        .bind(scan_id)
        .fetch_all(&self.pool)
        .await?;
        
        let stats = rows
            .iter()
            .map(|row| FileTypeStats {
                file_type: row.get(0),
                count: row.get(1),
                total_size: row.get(2),
                avg_confidence: row.get(3),
            })
            .collect();
        
        Ok(stats)
    }
    
    /// Close database connection pool
    pub async fn close(&self) -> Result<()> {
        self.pool.close().await;
        Ok(())
    }
}

// Database record types
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ScanRecord {
    pub scan_id: String,
    pub device_path: String,
    pub device_name: String,
    pub scan_start_time: i64,
    pub scan_end_time: Option<i64>,
    pub files_found: i32,
    pub is_completed: bool,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, sqlx::FromRow)]
pub struct ScanResultRecord {
    pub result_id: String,
    pub scan_id: String,
    pub file_type: String,
    pub estimated_size: i64,
    pub first_sector: i64,
    pub recovery_confidence: f32,
    pub fragmentation_level: f32,
    pub entropy: f32,
    pub status: String,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct RecoveryRecord {
    pub recovery_id: String,
    pub result_id: String,
    pub scan_id: String,
    pub destination_path: String,
    pub original_size: i64,
    pub recovered_size: i64,
    pub strategy: String,
    pub file_hash: String,
    pub integrity_status: String,
    pub integrity_score: f32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct RecoveryStats {
    pub total_files: i32,
    pub recovered_files: i32,
    pub total_size: i64,
    pub avg_confidence: f32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct FileTypeStats {
    pub file_type: String,
    pub count: i32,
    pub total_size: i64,
    pub avg_confidence: f32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ResultFilters {
    pub file_types: Option<Vec<String>>,
    pub min_confidence: Option<f32>,
    pub status: Option<String>,
    pub min_size: Option<i64>,
    pub max_size: Option<i64>,
}
```

## 17. METADATA MANAGEMENT ARCHITECTURE

### 17.1 Metadata Extraction & Storage

```rust
pub struct MetadataManager {
    db: Arc<Database>,
    extractors: Arc<Vec<Box<dyn MetadataExtractor>>>,
}

#[async_trait::async_trait]
pub trait MetadataExtractor: Send + Sync {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str>;
    async fn extract(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Metadata>;
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct Metadata {
    pub file_type: String,
    pub basic: BasicMetadata,
    pub specific: Option<SpecificMetadata>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct BasicMetadata {
    pub size: u64,
    pub created_date: Option<String>,
    pub modified_date: Option<String>,
    pub author: Option<String>,
    pub title: Option<String>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
#[serde(untagged)]
pub enum SpecificMetadata {
    Image(ImageMetadata),
    Document(DocumentMetadata),
    Video(VideoMetadata),
    Audio(AudioMetadata),
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ImageMetadata {
    pub width: Option<u32>,
    pub height: Option<u32>,
    pub color_space: Option<String>,
    pub dpi: Option<u32>,
    pub camera_make: Option<String>,
    pub camera_model: Option<String>,
    pub iso: Option<u16>,
    pub f_number: Option<f32>,
    pub focal_length: Option<f32>,
    pub exposure_time: Option<String>,
    pub gps_latitude: Option<f64>,
    pub gps_longitude: Option<f64>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct DocumentMetadata {
    pub page_count: Option<u32>,
    pub word_count: Option<u32>,
    pub character_count: Option<u32>,
    pub language: Option<String>,
    pub subject: Option<String>,
    pub keywords: Option<String>,
    pub producer: Option<String>,
    pub creator: Option<String>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct VideoMetadata {
    pub duration_ms: Option<u64>,
    pub width: Option<u32>,
    pub height: Option<u32>,
    pub fps: Option<f32>,
    pub bitrate: Option<u32>,
    pub codec: Option<String>,
    pub audio_tracks: Option<u32>,
    pub subtitle_tracks: Option<u32>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct AudioMetadata {
    pub duration_ms: Option<u64>,
    pub bitrate: Option<u32>,
    pub sample_rate: Option<u32>,
    pub channels: Option<u8>,
    pub codec: Option<String>,
    pub artist: Option<String>,
    pub album: Option<String>,
    pub genre: Option<String>,
    pub track_number: Option<u32>,
}

pub struct ImageMetadataExtractor;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl MetadataExtractor for ImageMetadataExtractor {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str> {
        vec!["JPEG", "PNG", "BMP", "GIF", "TIFF", "WebP", "RAW"]
    }
    
    async fn extract(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Metadata> {
        let basic = BasicMetadata {
            size: data.len() as u64,
            ..Default::default()
        };
        
        // Use image-rs to extract metadata
        let metadata = if let Ok(image) = image::load_from_memory(data) {
            let (width, height) = image.dimensions();
            Some(SpecificMetadata::Image(ImageMetadata {
                width: Some(width),
                height: Some(height),
                ..Default::default()
            }))
        } else {
            None
        };
        
        Ok(Metadata {
            file_type: "Image".to_string(),
            basic,
            specific: metadata,
        })
    }
}

pub struct DocumentMetadataExtractor;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl MetadataExtractor for DocumentMetadataExtractor {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str> {
        vec!["PDF", "DOCX", "DOC", "XLS", "XLSX", "PPT", "PPTX"]
    }
    
    async fn extract(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Metadata> {
        let basic = BasicMetadata {
            size: data.len() as u64,
            ..Default::default()
        };
        
        // Extract PDF metadata if applicable
        let metadata = if data.len() > 4 && &data[0..4] == b"%PDF" {
            // Parse PDF metadata
            Some(SpecificMetadata::Document(DocumentMetadata {
                page_count: Self::extract_pdf_page_count(data),
                ..Default::default()
            }))
        } else {
            None
        };
        
        Ok(Metadata {
            file_type: "Document".to_string(),
            basic,
            specific: metadata,
        })
    }
}

impl DocumentMetadataExtractor {
    fn extract_pdf_page_count(data: &[u8]) -> Option<u32> {
        // Find /Pages and /Count in PDF
        let search_term = b"/Count";
        
        for window in data.windows(search_term.len()) {
            if window == search_term {
                // Parse number after /Count
                for i in window.len()..std::cmp::min(window.len() + 20, data.len()) {
                    if data[i] >= b'0' && data[i] <= b'9' {
                        let num_str = String::from_utf8_lossy(
                            &data[i..std::cmp::min(i + 10, data.len())]
                        );
                        if let Ok(count) = num_str.split_whitespace()
                            .next()
                            .and_then(|s| s.parse::<u32>().ok()) {
                            return Some(count);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        None
    }
}

pub struct VideoMetadataExtractor;
#[async_trait::async_trait]
impl MetadataExtractor for VideoMetadataExtractor {
    fn supported_types(&self) -> Vec<&str> {
        vec!["MP4", "AVI", "MKV", "WebM", "MOV", "FLV"]
    }
    
    async fn extract(&self, data: &[u8]) 
        -> Result<Metadata> {
        let basic = BasicMetadata {
            size: data.len() as u64,
            ..Default::default()
        };
        
        // Parse MP4/MOV moov atom if present
        let metadata = if data.len() > 8 {
            // Look for moov atom
            if let Some(pos) = Self::find_atom(data, b"moov") {
                Some(SpecificMetadata::Video(VideoMetadata {
                    duration_ms: Self::extract_duration(data, pos),
                    width: Self::extract_dimensions(data, pos).map(|d| d.0),
                    height: Self::extract_dimensions(data, pos).map(|d| d.1),
                    ..Default::default()
                }))
            } else {
                None
            }
        } else {
            None
        };
        
        Ok(Metadata {
            file_type: "Video".to_string(),
            basic,
            specific: metadata,
        })
    }
}

impl VideoMetadataExtractor {
    fn find_atom(data: &[u8], atom_type: &[u8]) -> Option<usize> {
        data.windows(4)
            .position(|window| window == atom_type)
    }
    
    fn extract_duration(data: &[u8], moov_pos: usize) -> Option<u64> {
        // Simplified - would parse mvhd atom
        None
    }
    
    fn extract_dimensions(data: &[u8], moov_pos: usize) -> Option<(u32, u32)> {
        // Simplified - would parse tkhd atom
        None
    }
}

impl MetadataManager {
    pub fn new(db: Arc<Database>) -> Self {
        MetadataManager {
            db,
            extractors: Arc::new(vec![
                Box::new(ImageMetadataExtractor) as Box<dyn MetadataExtractor>,
                Box::new(DocumentMetadataExtractor),
                Box::new(VideoMetadataExtractor),
            ]),
        }
    }
    
    pub async fn extract_metadata(
        &self,
        file_data: &[u8],
        file_type: &str,
    ) -> Result<Metadata> {
        // Find appropriate extractor
        for extractor in self.extractors.iter() {
            if extractor.supported_types().contains(&file_type) {
                return extractor.extract(file_data).await;
            }
        }
        
        // Default metadata
        Ok(Metadata {
            file_type: file_type.to_string(),
            basic: BasicMetadata {
                size: file_data.len() as u64,
                ..Default::default()
            },
            specific: None,
        })
    }
    
    pub async fn store_metadata(
        &self,
        result_id: &str,
        metadata: &Metadata,
    ) -> Result<()> {
        let metadata_json = serde_json::to_string(metadata)?;
        
        // Store in database (would add metadata table)
        // sqlx::query(
        //     "INSERT INTO file_metadata (result_id, metadata_json) VALUES (?, ?)"
        // )
        // .bind(result_id)
        // .bind(metadata_json)
        // .execute(&self.db.pool)
        // .await?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
}

impl Default for BasicMetadata {
    fn default() -> Self {
        BasicMetadata {
            size: 0,
            created_date: None,
            modified_date: None,
            author: None,
            title: None,
        }
    }
}

impl Default for ImageMetadata {
    fn default() -> Self {
        ImageMetadata {
            width: None,
            height: None,
            color_space: None,
            dpi: None,
            camera_make: None,
            camera_model: None,
            iso: None,
            f_number: None,
            focal_length: None,
            exposure_time: None,
            gps_latitude: None,
            gps_longitude: None,
        }
    }
}

impl Default for DocumentMetadata {
    fn default() -> Self {
        DocumentMetadata {
            page_count: None,
            word_count: None,
            character_count: None,
            language: None,
            subject: None,
            keywords: None,
            producer: None,
            creator: None,
        }
    }
}

impl Default for VideoMetadata {
    fn default() -> Self {
        VideoMetadata {
            duration_ms: None,
            width: None,
            height: None,
            fps: None,
            bitrate: None,
            codec: None,
```
