## 27. MONITORING & LOGGING SYSTEMS

### 27.1 Structured Logging with Tracing

```rust
use tracing::{info, warn, error, debug, span, Level};
use tracing_subscriber::{fmt, prelude::*, EnvFilter};
use tracing_appender::non_blocking;

pub fn initialize_logging(log_level: &str) -> Result<()> {
    // Create file appender
    let file_appender = tracing_appender::rolling::daily("./logs", "filerestorer.log");
    let (non_blocking, _guard) = non_blocking(file_appender);
    
    // Create console layer
    let console_layer = fmt::layer()
        .with_writer(std::io::stdout)
        .with_thread_ids(true)
        .with_thread_names(true)
        .with_target(true);
    
    // Create file layer
    let file_layer = fmt::layer()
        .with_writer(non_blocking)
        .json()
        .with_thread_ids(true);
    
    // Create filter
    let env_filter = EnvFilter::try_from_default_env()
        .unwrap_or_else(|_| EnvFilter::new(log_level));
    
    // Combine layers
    tracing_subscriber::registry()
        .with(env_filter)
        .with(console_layer)
        .with(file_layer)
	.init();
	Ok(())
}

pub struct LogContext {
    pub request_id: String,
    pub user_id: Option<String>,
    pub operation: String,
}

pub macro_rules! log_operation {
    ($level:expr, $op:expr, $msg:expr) => {
        let span = span!($level, $op, operation = $op);
        let _enter = span.enter();
        tracing::event!($level, $msg);
    };
}

pub struct PerformanceMetrics {
    pub operation: String,
    pub duration_ms: u64,
    pub bytes_processed: u64,
    pub success: bool,
}

impl PerformanceMetrics {
    pub fn log(&self) {
        let throughput_mbps = if self.duration_ms > 0 {
            (self.bytes_processed as f64 / 1_000_000.0) /
            (self.duration_ms as f64 / 1000.0)
        } else {
            0.0
        };
        
        info!(
            operation = %self.operation,
            duration_ms = self.duration_ms,
            bytes_processed = self.bytes_processed,
            throughput_mbps = throughput_mbps,
            success = self.success,
            "Operation completed"
        );
    }
}

pub struct RequestLogger {
    span: tracing::Span,
}

impl RequestLogger {
    pub fn new(request_id: &str, method: &str, path: &str) -> Self {
        let span = span!(
            Level::INFO,
            "request",
            request_id = request_id,
            method = method,
            path = path
        );
        
        RequestLogger { span }
    }
    
    pub fn log_response(&self, status: u16, duration_ms: u64) {
        let _enter = self.span.enter();
        info!(
            status = status,
            duration_ms = duration_ms,
            "Request completed"
        );
    }
    
    pub fn log_error(&self, error: &str) {
        let _enter = self.span.enter();
        error!(error = error, "Request failed");
    }
}
```

### 27.2 Metrics & Observability

```rust
use prometheus::{
    Counter, Histogram, Gauge, Registry,
    HistogramOpts, CounterOpts, GaugeOpts,
};
use std::sync::Arc;

pub struct MetricsCollector {
    // Scan metrics
    pub scans_initiated: Counter,
    pub scans_completed: Counter,
    pub scans_failed: Counter,
    pub scan_duration: Histogram,
    pub files_detected: Counter,
    
    // Recovery metrics
    pub recoveries_initiated: Counter,
    pub recoveries_completed: Counter,
    pub recoveries_failed: Counter,
    pub recovery_duration: Histogram,
    pub bytes_recovered: Counter,
    
    // System metrics
    pub active_scans: Gauge,
    pub active_recoveries: Gauge,
    pub device_scan_speed_mbps: Gauge,
    pub cache_hit_rate: Gauge,
    pub database_operations: Counter,
    pub database_errors: Counter,
    pub database_latency: Histogram,
    
    // Security metrics
    pub auth_attempts: Counter,
    pub auth_failures: Counter,
    pub auth_lockouts: Counter,
    pub encryption_operations: Counter,
    pub audit_logs_written: Counter,
    
    registry: Arc<Registry>,
}

impl MetricsCollector {
    pub fn new() -> Result<Self> {
        let registry = Arc::new(Registry::new());
        
        // Initialize all metrics
        let scans_initiated = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_scans_initiated_total",
                "Total number of scans initiated")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(scans_initiated.clone()))?;
        
        let scans_completed = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_scans_completed_total",
                "Total number of scans completed successfully")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(scans_completed.clone()))?;
        
        let scans_failed = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_scans_failed_total",
                "Total number of failed scans")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(scans_failed.clone()))?;
        
        let scan_duration = Histogram::with_opts(
            HistogramOpts::new("filerestorer_scan_duration_seconds",
                "Scan operation duration in seconds")
                .buckets(vec![
                    10.0, 30.0, 60.0, 120.0, 300.0, 600.0, 1800.0, 3600.0
                ])
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(scan_duration.clone()))?;
        
        let files_detected = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_files_detected_total",
                "Total number of files detected")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(files_detected.clone()))?;
        
        let recoveries_initiated = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_recoveries_initiated_total",
                "Total number of recovery operations initiated")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(recoveries_initiated.clone()))?;
        
        let recoveries_completed = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_recoveries_completed_total",
                "Total number of recovery operations completed")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(recoveries_completed.clone()))?;
        
        let recoveries_failed = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_recoveries_failed_total",
                "Total number of failed recovery operations")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(recoveries_failed.clone()))?;
        
        let recovery_duration = Histogram::with_opts(
            HistogramOpts::new("filerestorer_recovery_duration_seconds",
                "Recovery operation duration in seconds")
                .buckets(vec![
                    1.0, 5.0, 10.0, 30.0, 60.0, 300.0, 600.0
                ])
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(recovery_duration.clone()))?;
        
        let bytes_recovered = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_bytes_recovered_total",
                "Total bytes recovered")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(bytes_recovered.clone()))?;
        
        let active_scans = Gauge::with_opts(
            GaugeOpts::new("filerestorer_active_scans",
                "Number of currently active scans")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(active_scans.clone()))?;
        
        let active_recoveries = Gauge::with_opts(
            GaugeOpts::new("filerestorer_active_recoveries",
                "Number of currently active recovery operations")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(active_recoveries.clone()))?;
        
        let device_scan_speed_mbps = Gauge::with_opts(
            GaugeOpts::new("filerestorer_device_scan_speed_mbps",
                "Current device scan speed in MB/s")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(device_scan_speed_mbps.clone()))?;
        
        let cache_hit_rate = Gauge::with_opts(
            GaugeOpts::new("filerestorer_cache_hit_rate",
                "Cache hit rate (0-1)")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(cache_hit_rate.clone()))?;
        
        let database_operations = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_database_operations_total",
                "Total database operations")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(database_operations.clone()))?;
        
        let database_errors = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_database_errors_total",
                "Total database errors")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(database_errors.clone()))?;
        
        let database_latency = Histogram::with_opts(
            HistogramOpts::new("filerestorer_database_latency_ms",
                "Database operation latency in milliseconds")
                .buckets(vec![1.0, 5.0, 10.0, 50.0, 100.0, 500.0])
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(database_latency.clone()))?;
        
        let auth_attempts = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_auth_attempts_total",
                "Total authentication attempts")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(auth_attempts.clone()))?;
        
        let auth_failures = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_auth_failures_total",
                "Total authentication failures")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(auth_failures.clone()))?;
        
        let auth_lockouts = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_auth_lockouts_total",
                "Total authentication lockouts")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(auth_lockouts.clone()))?;
        
        let encryption_operations = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_encryption_operations_total",
                "Total encryption/decryption operations")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(encryption_operations.clone()))?;
        
        let audit_logs_written = Counter::with_opts(
            CounterOpts::new("filerestorer_audit_logs_written_total",
                "Total audit log entries written")
        )?;
        registry.register(Box::new(audit_logs_written.clone()))?;
        
        Ok(MetricsCollector {
            scans_initiated,
            scans_completed,
            scans_failed,
            scan_duration,
            files_detected,
            recoveries_initiated,
            recoveries_completed,
            recoveries_failed,
            recovery_duration,
            bytes_recovered,
            active_scans,
            active_recoveries,
            device_scan_speed_mbps,
            cache_hit_rate,
            database_operations,
            database_errors,
            database_latency,
            auth_attempts,
            auth_failures,
            auth_lockouts,
            encryption_operations,
            audit_logs_written,
            registry,
        })
    }
    
    pub fn get_metrics(&self) -> Result<String> {
        use prometheus::TextEncoder;
        let encoder = TextEncoder::new();
        encoder.encode_to_string(&self.registry.gather(), &mut Vec::new())
            .map_err(|e| format!("Failed to encode metrics: {}", e).into())
    }
}

// Metrics middleware for Actix
pub async fn metrics_handler(
    metrics: web::Data<Arc<MetricsCollector>>,
) -> HttpResponse {
    match metrics.get_metrics() {
        Ok(metrics_output) => {
            HttpResponse::Ok()
                .content_type("text/plain; charset=utf-8")
                .body(metrics_output)
        }
        Err(_) => {
            HttpResponse::InternalServerError().finish()
        }
    }
}
```

### 27.3 Alerting & Health Checks

```rust
pub struct HealthChecker {
    db: Arc<Database>,
    cache: Arc<CacheManager>,
    metrics: Arc<MetricsCollector>,
}

#[derive(Serialize)]
pub struct HealthStatus {
    pub status: String,
    pub timestamp: String,
    pub components: ComponentStatus,
    pub metrics: HealthMetrics,
}

#[derive(Serialize)]
pub struct ComponentStatus {
    pub database: ComponentHealth,
    pub cache: ComponentHealth,
    pub storage: ComponentHealth,
    pub encryption: ComponentHealth,
}

#[derive(Serialize)]
pub struct ComponentHealth {
    pub status: String,
    pub latency_ms: Option<u64>,
    pub error: Option<String>,
}

#[derive(Serialize)]
pub struct HealthMetrics {
    pub uptime_secs: u64,
    pub active_scans: i32,
    pub active_recoveries: i32,
    pub cache_hit_rate: f32,
}

impl HealthChecker {
    pub fn new(
        db: Arc<Database>,
        cache: Arc<CacheManager>,
        metrics: Arc<MetricsCollector>,
    ) -> Self {
        HealthChecker { db, cache, metrics }
    }
    
    pub async fn check(&self) -> HealthStatus {
        let start = std::time::Instant::now();
        
        // Check database
        let db_status = self.check_database().await;
        
        // Check cache
        let cache_status = self.check_cache().await;
        
        // Check storage
        let storage_status = self.check_storage().await;
        
        // Check encryption
        let encryption_status = self.check_encryption().await;
        
        let overall_status = if db_status.status == "healthy"
            && cache_status.status == "healthy"
            && storage_status.status == "healthy" {
            "healthy".to_string()
        } else if db_status.status == "unhealthy"
            || cache_status.status == "unhealthy"
            || storage_status.status == "unhealthy" {
            "unhealthy".to_string()
        } else {
            "degraded".to_string()
        };
        
        HealthStatus {
            status: overall_status,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now().to_rfc3339(),
            components: ComponentStatus {
                database: db_status,
                cache: cache_status,
                storage: storage_status,
                encryption: encryption_status,
            },
            metrics: HealthMetrics {
                uptime_secs: start.elapsed().as_secs(),
                active_scans: 0,
                active_recoveries: 0,
                cache_hit_rate: 0.0,
            },
        }
    }
    
    async fn check_database(&self) -> ComponentHealth {
        let start = std::time::Instant::now();
        
        // Perform health check query
        match self.db.health_check().await {
            Ok(_) => ComponentHealth {
                status: "healthy".to_string(),
                latency_ms: Some(start.elapsed().as_millis() as u64),
                error: None,
            },
            Err(e) => ComponentHealth {
                status: "unhealthy".to_string(),
                latency_ms: Some(start.elapsed().as_millis() as u64),
                error: Some(e.to_string()),
            },
        }
    }
    
    async fn check_cache(&self) -> ComponentHealth {
        let start = std::time::Instant::now();
        
        // Test cache put/get
        match self.cache.put("health_check".to_string(), vec![0u8; 100]).await {
            Ok(_) => {
                match self.cache.get("health_check").await {
                    Ok(Some(_)) => ComponentHealth {
                        status: "healthy".to_string(),
                        latency_ms: Some(start.elapsed().as_millis() as u64),
                        error: None,
                    },
                    _ => ComponentHealth {
                        status: "degraded".to_string(),
                        latency_ms: Some(start.elapsed().as_millis() as u64),
                        error: Some("Cache retrieval failed".to_string()),
                    },
                }
            }
            Err(e) => ComponentHealth {
                status: "unhealthy".to_string(),
                latency_ms: Some(start.elapsed().as_millis() as u64),
                error: Some(e.to_string()),
            },
        }
    }
    
    async fn check_storage(&self) -> ComponentHealth {
        // Check if storage is accessible
        ComponentHealth {
            status: "healthy".to_string(),
            latency_ms: Some(0),
            error: None,
        }
    }
    
    async fn check_encryption(&self) -> ComponentHealth {
        // Test encryption/decryption
        ComponentHealth {
            status: "healthy".to_string(),
            latency_ms: Some(0),
            error: None,
        }
    }
}

pub async fn health_check_handler(
    checker: web::Data<Arc<HealthChecker>>,
) -> HttpResponse {
    let status = checker.check().await;
    
    let status_code = match status.status.as_str() {
        "healthy" => actix_web::http::StatusCode::OK,
        "degraded" => actix_web::http::StatusCode::OK,
        _ => actix_web::http::StatusCode::SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,
    };
    
    HttpResponse::build(status_code).json(status)
}
```

## 28. CONFIGURATION MANAGEMENT

### 28.1 Configuration System

```rust
use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};
use config::{Config, ConfigError, File, Environment};
use std::path::Path;

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct AppConfig {
    pub server: ServerConfig,
    pub database: DatabaseConfig,
    pub cache: CacheConfig,
    pub security: SecurityConfig,
    pub logging: LoggingConfig,
    pub scanning: ScanningConfig,
    pub recovery: RecoveryConfig,
    pub cloud: CloudConfig,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ServerConfig {
    pub host: String,
    pub port: u16,
    pub workers: usize,
    pub timeout_secs: u64,
    pub max_request_size: u64,
    pub enable_https: bool,
    pub cert_path: Option<String>,
    pub key_path: Option<String>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct DatabaseConfig {
    pub url: String,
    pub max_connections: u32,
    pub connection_timeout_secs: u64,
    pub query_timeout_secs: u64,
    pub enable_migrations: bool,
    pub backup_enabled: bool,
    pub backup_interval_hours: u32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct CacheConfig {
    pub l1_max_size: usize,
    pub l1_ttl_secs: u64,
    pub l2_max_entries: usize,
    pub l2_ttl_secs: u64,
    pub enable_compression: bool,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct SecurityConfig {
    pub jwt_secret: String,
    pub jwt_expiry_hours: i64,
    pub encryption_algorithm: String,
    pub key_derivation_iterations: u32,
    pub rate_limit_attempts: u32,
    pub rate_limit_window_secs: u64,
    pub cors_allowed_origins: Vec<String>,
    pub require_https: bool,
    pub security_headers_enabled: bool,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct LoggingConfig {
    pub level: String,
    pub format: String, // json, text
    pub output: String, // stdout, file, both
    pub file_path: String,
    pub max_file_size_mb: u64,
    pub max_backups: u32,
    pub enable_metrics: bool,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ScanningConfig {
    pub default_scan_type: String, // quick, normal, deep
    pub parallel_threads: usize,
    pub read_ahead_sectors: usize,
    pub max_scan_duration_hours: u32,
    pub enable_smart_scan: bool,
    pub signature_database_update_interval_days: u32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct RecoveryConfig {
    pub default_destination: String,
    pub verify_integrity: bool,
    pub enable_auto_repair: bool,
    pub parallel_recoveries: usize,
    pub retry_failed_sectors: bool,
    pub max_retry_attempts: u32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct CloudConfig {
    pub enabled: bool,
    pub provider: String, // aws, azure, gcp
    pub bucket_name: String,
    pub region: String,
    pub access_key: String,
    pub secret_key: String,
    pub encryption_enabled: bool,
}

pub struct ConfigManager;

impl ConfigManager {
    pub fn load(env: &str) -> Result<AppConfig> {
        let config = Config::builder()
            // Load from config files
            .add_source(File::from(Path::new("config/default.toml")))
            .add_source(
                File::from(Path::new(&format!("config/{}.toml", env)))
                    .required(false)
            )
            // Load from environment variables
            .add_source(Environment::with_prefix("FILERESTORER"))
            .build()?;
        
        config.try_deserialize::<AppConfig>()
            .map_err(|e| format!("Config error: {}", e).into())
    }
    
    pub fn validate(config: &AppConfig) -> Result<()> {
        // Validate server config
        if config.server.port == 0 {
            return Err("Invalid server port".into());
        }
        
        // Validate database config
        if config.database.url.is_empty() {
            return Err("Database URL must be provided".into());
        }
        
        // Validate security config
        if config.security.jwt_secret.len() < 32 {
            return Err("JWT secret must be at least 32 characters".into());
        }
        
        // Validate cache config
        if config.cache.l1_max_size == 0 {
            return Err("Cache size must be > 0".into());
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
}

// Example configuration file (config/default.toml)
```

## 29. RELEASE MANAGEMENT

### 29.1 Release Pipeline

```rust
use semver::Version;
use std::process::Command;

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ReleaseInfo {
    pub version: Version,
    pub commit_hash: String,
    pub timestamp: String,
    pub changelog: String,
    pub build_artifacts: Vec<BuildArtifact>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct BuildArtifact {
    pub platform: String,
    pub file_path: String,
    pub checksum: String,
    pub size_bytes: u64,
}

pub struct ReleaseManager {
    project_root: std::path::PathBuf,
}

impl ReleaseManager {
    pub fn new(project_root: std::path::PathBuf) -> Self {
        ReleaseManager { project_root }
    }
    
    /// Bump version in Cargo.toml
    pub fn bump_version(&self, bump_type: &str) -> Result<Version> {
        // Read current version
        let cargo_toml_path = self.project_root.join("Cargo.toml");
        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&cargo_toml_path)?;
        
        // Parse version
        let mut version: Version = regex::Regex::new(r#"version = "([^"]+)""#)?
            .captures(&content)
            .ok_or("Version not found in Cargo.toml")?
            .get(1)
            .ok_or("Could not extract version")?
            .as_str()
            .parse()?;
        
        // Bump version
        match bump_type {
            "major" => version.major += 1,
            "minor" => {
                version.minor += 1;
                version.patch = 0;
            }
            "patch" => version.patch += 1,
            _ => return Err("Invalid bump type".into()),
        }
        
        // Update Cargo.toml
        let new_content = content.replace(
            &format!(r#"version = "{}"#, version),
            &format!(r#"version = "{}""#, version),
        );
        std::fs::write(&cargo_toml_path, new_content)?;
        
        Ok(version)
    }
    
    /// Create a release build
    pub fn create_release(&self, version: &Version) -> Result<ReleaseInfo> {
        // Get commit hash
        let commit_hash = self.get_commit_hash()?;
        
        // Build all targets
        let builder = Builder::new(self.project_root.clone());
        let artifacts = builder.build_all_targets()?;
        
        // Create build artifacts with checksums
        let build_artifacts: Result<Vec<_>> = artifacts
            .iter()
            .map(|(platform, path)| {
                let checksum = self.calculate_sha256(path)?;
                let metadata = std::fs::metadata(path)?;
                
                Ok(BuildArtifact {
                    platform: format!("{:?}", platform),
                    file_path: path.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
                    checksum,
                    size_bytes: metadata.len(),
                })
            })
            .collect();
        
        Ok(ReleaseInfo {
            version: version.clone(),
            commit_hash,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now().to_rfc3339(),
            changelog: self.generate_changelog(version)?,
            build_artifacts: build_artifacts?,
        })
    }
    
    pub fn publish_release(&self, release: &ReleaseInfo) -> Result<()> {
        // Create GitHub release
        self.create_github_release(release)?;
        
        // Upload to package registry
        self.publish_to_crates_io(release)?;
        
        // Upload artifacts to S3
        self.upload_artifacts_to_s3(release)?;
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn get_commit_hash(&self) -> Result<String> {
        let output = Command::new("git")
            .arg("rev-parse")
            .arg("HEAD")
            .current_dir(&self.project_root)
            .output()?;
        
        Ok(String::from_utf8(output.stdout)?
            .trim()
            .to_string())
    }
    
    fn calculate_sha256(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<String> {
        use sha2::{Sha256, Digest};
        use std::io::Read;
        
        let mut file = std::fs::File::open(path)?;
        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();
        let mut buffer = [0; 8192];
        
        loop {
            let n = file.read(&mut buffer)?;
            if n == 0 {
                break;
            }
            hasher.update(&buffer[..n]);
        }
        
        Ok(format!("{:x}", hasher.finalize()))
    }
    
    fn generate_changelog(&self, version: &Version) -> Result<String> {
        // Get commits since last release
        let output = Command::new("git")
            .arg("log")
            .arg(&format!("v{:?}..HEAD", version))
            .arg("--oneline")
            .current_dir(&self.project_root)
            .output()?;
        
        Ok(String::from_utf8(output.stdout)?)
    }
    
    fn create_github_release(&self, release: &ReleaseInfo) -> Result<()> {
        // Use GitHub API to create release
        // Would require GitHub token
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn publish_to_crates_io(&self, release: &ReleaseInfo) -> Result<()> {
        let output = Command::new("cargo")
            .arg("publish")
            .current_dir(&self.project_root)
            .output()?;
        
        if !output.status.success() {
            return Err(format!(
                "Failed to publish to crates.io: {}",
                String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stderr)
            ).into());
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn upload_artifacts_to_s3(&self, release: &ReleaseInfo) -> Result<()> {
        // Would upload to S3 bucket
        Ok(())
    }
}
```

```rust
use std::path::PathBuf;

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct BackupPlan {
    pub id: String,
    pub name: String,
    pub enabled: bool,
    pub schedule: BackupSchedule,
    pub retention: RetentionPolicy,
    pub target_destinations: Vec<BackupDestination>,
    pub exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
    pub compression_enabled: bool,
    pub encryption_enabled: bool,
    pub last_backup: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
    pub last_successful_backup: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
    pub last_failed_backup: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum BackupSchedule {
    Once,
    Hourly,
    Daily { hour: u32, minute: u32 },
    Weekly { day: u32, hour: u32, minute: u32 },
    Monthly { day: u32, hour: u32, minute: u32 },
    Custom(String), // Cron expression
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]

    pub keep_last_n: Option<u32>,

}

        path: String,

}

        use tokio::io::AsyncReadExt;
        
        let mut file = tokio::fs::File::open(path).await?;
        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();
```
